Well, no- She did. But in a different sense. Not on a trip away so soon. 

 

“Right..” Rio nodded, looking down as she pushed the hair out of her face, rasping a low- “What uh..time is it?” 

 

Agatha glanced over at her phone, not looking at Rio over her shoulder as she answered the question. “Close to five”

 

Rio grumbled, covering her face as she realized Nicky had been home alone for nearly a whole night. He wasn’t used to Rio being away overnight, let alone a few hours. And she hadn’t even asked Wanda to stop by like she typically would. 

 

I’m not a bad dog mom. I don’t ever do this. Rio told herself.  

 

As much as she wanted to stay till Agatha had to walk out the door, she needed to be responsible. It wasn’t fair to Nicky if she left him longer than she already had. Besides, her anxiety was crawling up her skin like a bug. Skin tingling, nerves bubbling..

 

I need to get home. 

 

Rio pushed the covers off, suddenly feeling exposed as her legs remained bare. Her skin was decorated in goosebumps, bruises, red marks. All of them like tattoos with Agatha as her artist. 

 

Agatha must’ve sensed her, maybe heard the ruffling of the covers behind because before Rio knew it-

 

“Here” 

 

A fresh pair of clothes were neatly folded. A pair of sweatpants, fresh underwear, and a sweater Agatha had retired years ago. Rio felt warm at the reminder of its existence. The brown wool one that hung loosely on her shoulders. 

 

Any other time, Rio would feel honored to wear her clothes. Pieces of her wardrobe Agatha probably didn’t care to remember, but Rio did. However, it felt different. She felt rushed, pushed out of Agatha’s home as if she was never welcomed hours ago. 

 

“Thank you..” She whispered. 

 

Agatha hummed, oblivious to Rio’s nerves as she spun around to continue packing. She tossed over her shoulder a low, 

 

“Much rather keep you without clothes on, but..” She looked over with a small wink. “I suppose I won’t be too selfish”

 

She turned back around right after saying it. The atmosphere turned colder. Rio felt a weird sinking feeling in her stomach, her heart thundering with every second that passed. 

 

It had to be herself. Agatha was flirting, smirking, winking at her like nothing had changed. Yet the packing, sudden disappearance- Maybe more so, absence was the word. 

 

Regardless, Rio’s anxiety was kicked into overdrive. Something wasn’t right, but Rio couldn’t exactly pinpoint what it was. Not yet, anyway. 

 

Rio pulled the underwear and sweatpants on, adjusting the waistband as she looked around for her belongings. Agatha must’ve been watching her, making her jump with a small,

 

“Taking off already?” Agatha asked. 

 

She briefly looked over at her, finding Agatha lifting the suitcase onto the floor. Her eyes locked on Rio the entire time. 

 

Rio shrugged, gesturing to Agatha’s bag with a nod. “And you aren’t?”

 

The woman's words were clipped, every syllable was tight. With every word she spoke, Agatha felt her heart clench and stomach sick. It was clear her packing before Rio woke up was the wrong decision. Something she hadn't even thought about. 

 

Unless, she did think about it..that was Rio’s worry. 

 

Agatha sighed, shaking her head. “Rio-”

 

“When are you back?” 

 

Rio rushed the question, desperate to derail an argument and stop them while they were ahead. Or, was that just her mind going into overdrive? 

 

Don’t do this. 

 

Fuck, she had a bad habit of this. Wanda had called her out on it her entire life, for the most part. Her overthinking, sudden anxiety always won. She was strong until it came to her own mind. A demon that felt impossible to face. 

 

Once her mind decided something wasn’t right, it was hard to go against that decision. Therapy briefly helped years ago, but she stopped going when the woman she saw retired. Wanda had always been on her about finding a new one. Maybe if she had listened, Rio wouldn’t be going into overdrive. 

 

“Monday” Agatha said, pulling her lips back to bite down on them before asking. “Are you- Is everything okay?”

 

Rio huffed with a weak smile, shaking her head in hopes to hide her fear. “Yeah. Why wouldn’t it be?”

 

Agatha swallowed the nerves down, second guessing what a few hours ago meant for them. She couldn’t help but hear the pitch in Rio’s tone, how she appeared to be distant even in the same room as her. Not even two hours prior, Rio was in her arms- Safe, secure, tucked in as if she had no plans on going anywhere. And now? 

 

Rio was avoiding looking at Agatha as if the woman was a monster. She was in such a hurry to find her belongings, barely spoke more than a few words. And when she did speak? It felt cold. Rio had hated her before, but not this. 

 

Agatha took in a deep breath, grasping onto straws to stop what was going on. 

 

“Is..” Agatha started, but decided to take a shot in the dark for what was wrong. “Listen, I always pack at the last second. I was just trying to be a little bit ahead and Billy is always eager to leave like-”

 

“Agatha”

 

“You know how he is with plans and roadtrips. There’s a reason we all don’t let that kid go alone!” 

 

Agatha nervously laughed at the end. But, it was too late.

 

Rio held her phone, wallet, and keys. She faked a warm smile which felt worrisome. Agatha felt a terror strike as if this would be the last time Rio stood in front of her. Leaving one question to scream in her mind,

 

What is happening? 

 

“I’ll see you Monday,” Rio said, leaning over to kiss her cheek. “Text me when you get there, okay?”

 

Agatha didn’t have a chance to hold her, never able to verbalize a reply. Rio walked out of her room- No, raced away out the front door, leaving the woman frozen, stunned, confused behind her. 

 

Agatha’s hand was in the air. Her cheek cold from the small kiss Rio so graciously left her with. And as the door shut, a sudden darkness fell in the silence with only thoughts that started to scream through her mind. 

 

She regrets last night. 

This was all too soon. 

I shouldn’t have been packing, oh my god. 

What did I do?

This is why I never fucking open up like that- Idiot. She loves you? No. Oh my god. 

 

Agatha’s hands ran over her face as her heart began to race out of control- threatening to send her into a panic attack. The thoughts were relentless, making her sick with every word. She wasn’t sure what turn they had taken, but maybe (hopefully) there wasn’t one at all. 

 

It was late, Rio realized she had to take care of Nicky. She was tired, cranky- Sometimes Rio wasn’t a morning person. It could simply be that and Agatha was overthinking this entire situation. 

 

However, all it did was bring up the parts of her she worked on tirelessly to silence for so long. Thoughts, hesitations, doubts and worries piled on top of one another- Leaving her fucked seven ways to Sunday (Not in the way she’d prefer either).

 

She’d spent so much of her life avoiding others, never allowing herself to be loved or feel such an emotion. And just when she was on the surface of doing so? Something went wrong, terribly wrong. Agatha wasn’t sure what to do, but the one old habit started to grip and cling to her like poison-

 

Run. 

 

 

“Don’t tell me you’re skipping town on her..” Wanda said. 

 

Rio laughed, packing a bag as her body trembled. At the age of twenty two, she was experiencing heartbreak. The worst she swore would happen to her. A love so strong had broken. A bond that severed felt like the end of her life. 

 

“What else am I supposed to do?”

 

“I don’t know, wild thought- Talk to her!” Wanda exclaimed. “What is running off even going to do?” 

 

“I’m not running off-”

 

“You booked yourself a last minute gig at a summer camp- A religious one, actually”

 

“So?”

 

“You’re going to a Christian all girls camp to escape your ex-girlfriend for the summer. Does that not sound a little insane to you?” 

 

Rio paused, looking up with her head tilting side to side before a strong-

 

“Nope”  

 

She went to continue packing, but Wanda had reached over- ripping the duffle bag to toss it on the floor. The clothes scattered out, but that wasn’t the frustrating part. Wanda made an effort to make a small rip in the opening so Rio would struggle to close it.

 

“What the fuck?!” Rio exclaimed. “That bag wasn’t cheap, you know?”

 

Wanda shrugged, slouching back into the couch with arms crossed tight against her chest. She didn’t care if Rio was pissed. She didn’t give a flying fuck if Rio would crash out, scream, call her every insult and name in the book. 

 

“You need therapy, Rio” 

 

Wanda said it as if it was nothing. A fact, words she had been saying to Rio for years now. Of course, her friend had been a wall to that fact. Not hearing her at all. Wanda could tell her till she was blue in the face and Rio still would do her own thing. 

 

“Not some preaching Jesus camp with bible thumping bonfires and prayers before every meal. Not even that can change or fix this!”

 

“We don’t know that”

 

“What? Are you praying they turn you straight because lemme’ tell you, Rio. Men aren’t any easier than women”

 

Rio didn’t look up or respond. Too busy picking up her clothes, assessing the damage Wanda did to her bag. 

 

“Is this really what you want for the rest of your life?” 

 

“A friend who breaks my bags? No, not really”

 

Wanda rolled her eyes. “You’re going to regret this one day. A woman is going to come along, you’re going to do this, and regret it” 

 

Rio huffed, muttering under her breath, “Bullshit”

 

“Yes. What you do is bullshit, honey. Very aware of tha-”

 

“What makes you so high and mighty? Huh?” 

 

Rio whipped around, arms thrown out with a glare stronger than her own pain. Deep down, logically, she knew Wanda only had her best interest at heart. But, the timing sucked. How repetitive her advice was becoming. A circle that never ended. 

 

“Have you ever considered I don’t need therapy and you’re just fucking putting that on me because you need-”

 

“Projecting. That’s called projecting”

 

“Oh my god!” Rio laughed, tossing the bag as she stormed to find a different one. “I feel like you going to college to be a fucking shrink has turned you into an asshole”

 

Wanda shook her head, voice wavering as she spoke, “That’s not fair. I’m just trying to help”

 

“Yeah, well- Maybe I don’t need it!” Rio yelled out. “I never asked-”

 

“God forbid I care about my best friend’s happiness”

 

“I never asked-”

 

“One day, Rio” Wanda stood, pointing a finger at her as she collected her belongings. “One day you’ll do this, sit with it, and realize how it’s not worth-”

 

“What makes you think I'll ever date again? Maybe I just want to grow old alone” 

 

Wanda stared, not buying her bullshit for a second. It may take years, possibly decades at worst. But Wanda knew Rio wasn't going to be alone. 

 

“Someone is out there-”

 

Rio scoffed, shaking her head with a grin filled with disgust. 

 

“And you need to fix your childish ways now before you're too old to do this” 

 

“And if I don't?” 

 

Rio had turned back around as she asked the question. Arms tossed to the side, voice softening into defeat. 

 

“Like I said,” Wanda stood taller with a little shrug. “You'll regret it” 

 

That memory played in Rio's head as she opened the kitchen door to let Nicky into the yard. Silently apologizing for abandoning him hours before.

 

No matter how hard she tried to stop the thought, scene, repetition in her mind- It played on repeat. Even if she was in her early twenties when it happened, the words felt fresh. They represented, related to what was going on in the present day. 

 

Therapy followed the memory. Years after that fight, she agreed and had gone to one session. Someone Wanda met during college and who she recommended off the bat when Rio gave in to the advice. 

 

“Instead of running- Why not stay?” 

 

Rio remembered sitting on the leather couch. The fabric had a few tears on the arm, clear people had picked at it over time. 

 

“Easier said than done, I know” She added. “But..how far can you run until you become too exhausted to exist?” 

 

As she grabbed the cup of kibble, dumping it into Nicky's bowl- Rio silently cursed herself out for thinking about it. 

 

Why can't my brain just shut the fuck up? 

 

The cycle from years ago was repeating itself. Clothes in a dryer, tossing in messy circles over and over. 

 

And she knew..it wasn’t worth it. Not when she went through hating Agatha to professing love on her doorstep. Not after finally allowing herself to be with someone more than just a meaningless way to pass the time or a pathetic attempt at not being alone. 

 

What’s the worst that can happen? 

 

Don't answer that . Rio told herself. 

 

But, seriously- What is the worst that can happen? 

 

Rio had been unhappy for years. That feeling wasn't anything new. She was familiar with it, able to survive the loneliness before and would after the saga of Agatha Harkness in her life. 

 

Shorter than the fuckin’ Twilight Saga.. Rio snickered in her mind. 

 

She turned the faucet off, bringing the bowl of cold water to place next to the food. Rio brushed her hands off as she stepped to the door. A soft whistle with a little, 

 

“Nicky, come eat bud!” 

 

He flipped around, jumping across the yard with his tail wagging to skid through the threshold. She chuckled, ruffling his hair before slipping by to find her phone. 

 

“Wish I had your energy, dude” Rio said over her shoulder. 

 

She found her phone tossed on the coffee table in the living room. Rio picked it up, silently hoping Agatha had called or texted- But there was nothing. 

 

She's busy packing and Billy probably showed up way too early..

 

Billy was a sweetheart, but filled with anxiety and Lilia joked he was made of OCD habits. Other professors and staff probably thought the few were too protective of him. But even Rio silently agreed it was best to keep him close. 

 

He grew up in foster homes, bouncing between them his entire life. Rio got the whole story in the break room his second month there. Not that she ever asked, but it was clear he needed to say all of it. 

 

She silently adored as well how Agatha was really the one to take him under her wing. The last trip to see his brother up north he made was alone. Agatha ended up leaving work early to rescue him in the mountains. 

 

His car skidded off the road covered in ice, landing in a ditch. Luckily a tree was there to catch his fall before tumbling down the mountain completely. No one let him travel alone after that incident. At least, Agatha never would. 

 

He was known to be chronically early for everything. Hence why Agatha was most likely packing before Rio woke-

 

Shit. 

 

Rio closed her eyes, rubbing a hand over her face as reality seriously sank into her bones. She overreacted. Of fucking course, she overreacted. Her anxiety won and had gotten the best of her. 

 

God, I'm an idiot…and maybe I need to go back to therapy. 

 

She forced herself to pull up her messages with Agatha. The last few being stupid selfies they had sent to each other during the day. 

 

One of Agatha sneaking into Rio's classroom, pretending to bite her plant. The next was Rio cleaning it with the caption, 

 

“Gross” 

 

While Agatha replied with smirking emojis and a quick, 

 

“You don't say that when my mouth is elsewhere..”

 

God, she hated how perfect the woman was for her. Cheeky, annoying, sarcastic and beautiful all at the same time. Maybe that didn't help her anxiety though. 

 

How can she even want me? Rio wondered. 

 

Regardless, her thumbs moved to type a small message. A quick little goodbye with a small joke in between. How she hoped they had a good trip, Nicky missed her…and maybe she did too. 

 

She hit send and let go of the breath that lived in her chest for far too long. 

 

That had to show Agatha everything was fine, right? Rio tossed her phone back on the coffee table, debating a quick shower- However, she didn't want to rid Agatha's touch completely. But on the same token? Showering was therapy. It'd ease her stress and worries more than sleep would. 

 

Fine. She could cover herself in Agatha once the woman was back home in a few days. Rio figured she had fixed whatever small damage had been done that morning with the text. 

 

Well…so she thought, anyway.

 

It was noon when Rio woke up from her nap on the couch. Nicky's head was tucked in her lap, an episode of Shark Tank played on the TV- Someone crying while giving their sob story. 

 

Rio didn't even watch for the products. She only watched to make fun of how people cried their eyes out for pity money. 

Another reason she had fallen in love with Agatha was because the woman did the same. 

 

They spent time cuddled on the couch, someone's legs over the other's lap. Both snickering and mocking the people on screen. And as Rio woke up…she realized how lonely the atmosphere was. Barely awake for a minute and that feeling punched her in the gut. 

 

She looked around frantically for her phone, hopeful and anxious to see what Agatha had replied. Usually it didn't take long for the woman to get back to her. At worst, two or three hours if she had lectures and students to help after class. 

 

And so it was safe to say when Rio swiped her phone screen, hopeful her notifications glitched-

 

Nothing.

 

Her heart sank, stomach twisted into a knot. She slowly put her phone down, tongue swiped on the inside of her cheek. 

 

Okay. 

It's fine. 

Billy probably didn't want to drive..or Agatha wasn't letting him. More that than anything. 

So, she's busy. It's fine. 

 

Everything. Is. Fine. 

 

(It was in fact, not fine) 

 

Rio started to chew the skin off her thumbnail. Her eyes locked to the screen, hopeful the show would take her attention and mind off of Agatha. She should have known that wouldn't work. 

 

Even before all this, Agatha Harkness lived rent free in Rio Vidal's mind. Since their first meeting, since every Christmas party, the first day back from summer vacation. All of it. 

 

“Are you really talking about Agatha again?” Wanda asked. 

 

Rio scoffed, scrunching her nose in disgust as she aggressively shook her head. 

 

“I'm saying how irritating she is’ 

 

Natasha snickered. “Irritating to the point you mention her daily-”

 

“I do not!” 

 

“Rio. It's the middle of July and you're bringing her up” Wanda pointed out. “You haven't seen her in weeks” 

 

Rio huffed, breath puffing out a silent words as she shook her head, eyes flickering between the two. They were filled with amusement, questions, ready to fire back with their own arguments left and right. 

 

She shook her head, denying what should be obvious. “I don't even like her” 

 

“Never said anything about liking” Natasha pointed out. “Just how you keep talking about her”

 

“Oh come on!” Rio laughed. “Do we not shit talk people we can't stand now?!” 

 

“Not like a broken record and as if she is the only thing you think about” Natasha said. 

 

Rio glared at her, whipping her head to find Wanda sipping from her iced tea. She shrugged, obviously not taking Rio's side in this. 

 

“Unbelievable..” She muttered. 

 

The woman grabbed her belongings in a rough manner. Muttering under her breath insults and words of how she hated them both. 

 

Natasha smirked, Wanda unable to control herself as she called after her-

 

“I expect you to talk about us 24/7 since you hate us, sweetie!” 

 

“Right?” Natasha laughed. 

 

Rio shook her head as she stormed out of their backyard, tossing over her shoulder in a childish manner, 

 

“I don't like her!” 

 

The gate slammed shut, leaving her friends giggling behind. 

 

“She so likes her” Natasha snorted. “When do you think she'll realize it?” 

 

Wanda sighed, pulling knees to her chest with a shrug. 

 

“One day..” She looked over at her wife with a sad smile. “If we're lucky” 

 

Natasha hummed. “It is amusing torturing her in the meantime though” 

 

“Oh, without a doubt” 

 

Back then, Rio could now admit she thought about Agatha excessively. Maybe more than she ever bargained for or admitted to. 

 

However, now? Since Agatha used to reside in her home, spend every minute they could together, made her smile and worshipped every inch of her? 

 

God, it was worse than ever. And this silence, the awkward tension from earlier that morning. Rio's anxiety taking over, making her overreact to something so small. She hadn't even let Agatha explain herself before taking off. 

 

Rio sat in silence for an extra twenty minutes. Her mind played Agatha on a loop. Like a broken record, DVD that kept skipping the same scene from hours ago. Typically, she'd continue being alone. Nicky usually made good enough company. 

 

But…this was too much. 

 

She checked her phone again to make sure Agatha still hadn't replied before abruptly getting up with a little apology to Nicky, but not one she really said. He would only be sad for a second because Rio had jumped up to grab his harness and leash. 

 

Instantly when the metal clinked, Nicky's paws ran across the floor. He jumped in the air, tail wagging as he spun in a circle. Even through her terrible thoughts, feeling of doom- Rio couldn't help but smile. 

 

“Wanna’ go see that annoying redhead you adore?” She asked. 

 

He whined as she adjusted the harness. A little laugh escaped her over the sound. 

 

“I'm going as fast as I can, dude. Cut a girl some slack, yeah?” 

 

Nicky chased off to the front door the second she clicked his leash on. She felt herself pulled, nearly going face first on the floorboards. That still wouldn't compare to what she felt in that moment with everything else going on. 

 

Rio slipped her slides on, thankful Wanda only lived a walking distance from her. She was not in the mood to drive. A walk always helped her ease her mind somewhat to begin with. 

 

She grabbed her wallet, made sure the phone was in the pocket before opening the front door and muttering, 

 

“We're about to never hear the end of this, buddy” 

 

Rio only barged in on Wanda with no warning when she was a wreck. The last time she did was when Nicky had gone missing. 

 

He had run off down the street, into someone's house and decided to have dinner with them. Luckily once they saw her Facebook post, she was contacted instantly. However, that was one of the only moments she showed up on Wanda's doorstep unannounced. And now that was going to happen because of fucking Agatha? 

 

Oh, she's going to be so annoying about this..

 

Though, Rio knew it was better than spiraling alone. Even if her best friend was about to drive her to the brink of insanity. 

 

 

Nicky knocked on the door for her. Well, more jumped and skidded his paws against the wood. Wanda had encouraged that in hopes it would, 

 

“Mark his existence. Create a memory and add love” 

 

While Natasha and Rio silently agreed to fix it if he ever left any damage. Sometimes Wanda was far too sentimental. 

 

She heard footsteps come closer to the door. The music blaring was turned down as the door opened, revealing Wanda in her cleaning clothes. Hair tied back, one rubber glove on with the other tossed over her shoulder on top of the damp towel. 

 

At first she was smiling, warmly greeting the stranger at the door. Though as she found Rio in a hoodie, eyes tired and already starting to gloss over- 

 

“Get in here” 

 

Wanda took the leash from Rio, guiding Nicky in first before holding the door open for her to follow. 

 

Rio shoved her hands in her pocket, head down as Nicky ran off to the living room. Mostly likely searching for Natasha who was on a business trip. Wanda would make up for his sadness by giving him treats later on when he realized she wasn't there. 

 

For now, the woman's focus was on Rio who was slugging her way to the kitchen. Her silence spoke volumes, telling Wanda this was definitely Agatha related. 

 

“What happened?” She asked from behind. 

 

Rio puffed out a laugh as she yanked the chair from the table, plopping in it with an exaggerated sigh. 

 

“Well, that sounds lovely!” Wanda chirped with a subtle glare. “Coffee?” She asked. 

 

Rio nodded. She brought one knee up to her chest, hugging it as she forced herself to check her phone and again-

 

Nothing. 

 

Wanda gave some grace to her, allowing the silence while making her cup of coffee. Other times, she'd add sugar and creamer- Maybe make up her own stupid, extra flavoring. But, right now? 

 

“K’,” Wanda slid the coffee mug over, dropping in the chair across from her. “Coffee is black as night” 

 

Rio looked over with a little smirk. 

 

“That easy to read?” 

 

Black coffee was Rio's go to when she was sad. She said once it was bitter, something to try and focus disgust on over her own life. Wanda thought it was stupid, but never one to argue someone's coping mechanism. 

 

“Well, you showed up on my door with no warning. You look like shit. Your eye bags are blacker than this coffee. Andddd, you sound like Death” 

 

Rio took a sip from the coffee, nodding a bit with a shrug. 

 

“Right on the money..” She muttered. 

 

“Per usual,” Wanda smiled. “Now. What's going on, sweetie?”

 

“Honestly” 

 

Rio sighed, putting the coffee down to run a hand through her hair. Elbow resting on her knee, looking up at Wanda with a sad smile. 

 

“I don’t know what’s going on”

 

Wanda narrowed her eyes, asking a low, “What did you do?” 

 

Rio huffed. “Why do you instantly think I did something?” 

 

“Because I know this face, this…demeanor of yours” 

 

Wanda wiggled her fingers up and down. She then pursed her lips, a hum while tapping her finger on her chin. Clearly digging herself in thought, analyzing Rio until she pointed-

 

“What did you overreact to?” 

 

Rio rolled her eyes, reconsidering if showing up on Wanda's doorstep was the right idea or not. 

 

“Oh, come on-”

 

“I'm right!” Wanda exclaimed. “You have a certain look to this”

 

“And what is that?” 

 

“Regret, despair, and upcoming anger with yourself that is due any minute now” 

 

Nicky broke the tension for a second, running in to cut Wanda's interrogation off. She chuckled softly, getting up to the cabinet for his cookies. 

 

“Figure out she's not here, huh?” Wanda asked. 

 

“He's beyond disappointed we have to put up with you” Rio said in a monotone voice. 

 

“Your mother acts like she wasn't the one to show up on my doorstep looking terrible” 

 

Wanda said in a baby voice to Nicky before leaning down to kiss his head, hand him the two cookies for him to run off with. Rio rolled her eyes, but softly smiled as she watched her boy chase off into the living room. Most likely would eat and then play with the toys they kept for him. 

 

She watched Wanda grab a new towel, picking up a plate from the strainer to dry it off before whipping back around. 

 

“Well?” She asked. “This is clearly Agatha related as well-”

 

“What are you? Some know it all freak?” 

 

Wanda snickered. “No, just cursed to know you since childhood” 

 

Rio sighed, taking another sip from her coffee before figuring out where to begin. 

 

“I uh..” She shrugged, looking around as she strung together words in a messy manner, “Imayhavetoldherilovedherthanranoutthismorningonher..” 

 

Wanda paused, holding onto the plate as she broke the words apart to make sense of them. Luckily over the years she learned how to break down Rio's one worded essays, muttered under her breath, barely comprehensive. 

 

Her jaw slightly dropped, nearly dropping the plate as she gasped, 

 

“Shut. Up!” 

 

She rushed over, dropping in her chair without a car as the plate almost broke on the table. 

 

Wanda grinned like a mad woman, leaning close as she gasped in a giddy manner, 

 

“You told her you loved her?! Oh my god, Rio! That's-”

 

“Did you not catch last part of that?” Rio asked. 

 

Wanda waved her hand. “I did and I'll address that in two seconds just-” 

 

She shook her head with a smile, voice softening as she spoke, 

 

“You love someone, Rio. To the point you confessed it! That's…huge! I'm so happy and-”

 

“I probably just fucked it all up” Rio laughed with a shake of her head. “New world record for that, huh?” 

 

Wanda's smile faded, but still somewhat remained. She didn't think for a second that she and Agatha were over. Not in the slightest. Wanda had called it years ago the two were more than enemies, not even friends. 

 

No matter what happened, Wanda was sure it wouldn't change the outcome. 

 

And also, she had just won twenty bucks from her wife that Rio finally confessed sooner than they took the bet on. It was hard to not keep some kind of smile. 

 

“What happened then? How did you ruin this?”

 

Rio took in a deep breath, cringing as the memory replayed in her mind again. This time, she'd have to vocalize it. Even in a short summary, it felt hopeless. A pain that grew stronger with worries piling on top of each other. 

 

The image of Agatha's face was clear. How confused and lost she appeared. The way she stuttered over her words. How she frantically searched to explain herself, but Rio had basically shunned her. Only offering a peck on her cheek before running off like Cinderella after midnight. 

 

She closed her eyes, hoping to hide in the darkness of her mind. It didn't work. Especially with Wanda before her. 

 

“Ri-”

 

“She was packing when I woke up” 

 

“Packing? For what?”

 

“Going up north with that Billy kid? He wants to see his brother and I've told you about him. No way Agatha would let him go alone” 

 

Wanda nodded. “Soooo, what does that have to do with the packing before you wake up? I don't get-”

 

“It was like she- I don't know. She gave me clothes” 

 

“And that was a bad thing?” 

 

“At the moment- Well, in that moment, yeah” 

 

Wanda was about to ask why, but heard it in Rio's voice why she viewed it in a negative light. She slowly nodded, leaning back in her chair with arms crossed against her chest. 

 

“You thought she was kicking you out..” 

 

Rio nodded. 

 

“Which only sent you into panic mode thinking you did something wrong and-”

 

“Then I ran out” Rio finished.

 

The woman sighed, running a hand over her red hair that was frizzed out- Slipping out of the hair tie that loosely held it back. 

 

She wasn't surprised to say the least. Rio had commonly drawn and jumped in the air to conclusions faster than the speed of light. Which always led her to be in positions like so. 

 

“Have you texted her?” 

 

Rio nodded. 

 

“And?” 

 

“Nothing” She shrugged, her voice small as she looked at her coffee. “Told you..fucked it up” 

 

Wanda sighed. Her voice sympathetic with eyes softer than a cloud, hoping to ease Rio's worries the best she could. Though that was never an easy task. Xanax sometimes barely touched Rio at all. 

 

“Honey, she's on a trip. I'm sure she's driving or busy” She said, shrugging with a quick- “You know how Natasha is! Sometimes she gets so wrapped up to reply or-”

 

“That's work though,” Rio said. “This is just a trip north. Few hours out. I won't blame her if she never speaks to me again. I basically fucked and ran” 

 

Wanda nodded, not arguing with her on that. She may try to relax, console, and make her friend feel better. 

 

However, Wanda was never the type of woman who would lie to you. She was blunt, especially with Rio. Still pointed out when the woman was in the wrong even at her worst. 

 

“Like you said though,” Wanda started. “That Billy- He sounds like a lovely boy, but a handful” She smiled. “I'm sure her focus is on surviving that trip with him in one piece” 

 

Rio shrugged. Maybe Wanda was right. Agatha did heavily focus on him sometimes when she was worried. And he hadn't traveled that far north since the car accident. He only took small trips, and hadn't left that far in a while. 

 

He was probably rambling nonstop. Agatha probably took over the wheel to avoid him having a panic attack when they got to the mountain he almost fell off of. 

 

“When did you last text her?” 

 

“Earlier like..” Rio picked her phone up, checking her phone to see- “Close to 6ish”

 

Nearly 6 hours since- Fuck. Fuck. Fuck! 

 

“Okay, hey..” Wanda reached out to take her phone aside. “Breathe”

 

As if she could read the inner monologue, hear the silent panic attack boiling up within her- Wanda went into action to bring her back down to earth. Hold her there till she could remain grounded on her own. 

 

“Again- Most likely busy. And doesn't he live up towards Lake Placid? Service is so sketchy up there, you know that” 

 

“But-”

 

“They probably stopped for lunch or rest” Wanda said. “Maybe his brother met them somewhere and they're busy”

 

“Wanda-”

 

“There are so many possible answers to this” She said. “Doubtful she's ignoring you. It's clear how obsessed that woman is with you!” 

 

Wanda smiled, not letting Rio try to argue before spilling into her view on Agatha. 

 

“Natasha and I spoke about her the rest of the night, you know?” She started. “The way she looks at you is insane , Rio. I swear, it was like some freaky protective love drunk look. And she just radiates life beside you. There's-”

 

“Did you not focus on the way she left though?” 

 

“No because I just won a bet with Natasha you'd be on her doorstep not long after, actually” 

 

Rio scoffed. “You assholes took bets? ”

 

Wanda rolled her eyes. 

 

“Okay, one” She held her finger up. “You and Natasha take bets on everything” 

 

Wanda sat up straighter, head held high with a smug grin. 

 

“Two, yes. In fact, I need you to tell her or sign a document this happened because she owes me a twenty and a new purse” 

 

Rio rolled her eyes. “You two are ridiculous”

 

“And so are you for not seeing how crazy Agatha is about you” Wanda said. “How you two were ever enemies, I'll never know”

 

“She was an ass to me the second we met!”

 

“And you've been a miserable asshole to her for years,” Wanda countered. “The only good part is Natasha never won the bet you'd start hate fucking years ago”

 

“There was another bet?!” Rio exclaimed in disbelief. “How many have you two had? Do you bet on my love life as a pass time for fun or something?!” 

 

Wanda ignored her completely, brushing her off to focus on what really mattered. The main topic they had to talk about, conquer, and get her best friend through this before she destroyed something good completely. 

 

“Try calling her?”

 

Rio rolled her eyes, Wanda scoffed. 

 

“Is that such a bad idea?”

 

“She isn’t even answering my texts”

 

“Oh, please. That isn’t even why you won’t do it”

 

“Wha-”

 

“Texting has always been easier than using your actual words, having to speak instead of having time to think thoroughly on what to say” Wanda shrugged. 

 

Rio shook her head. “Okay- No. If that were the case, I wouldn’t have been at her place last night. This is because she won’t answer me” 

 

“Or you’re worried about bothering her”

 

Rio leaned back in defeat, hating how Wanda was right (Per fuckin’ usual, but Rio would never admit that outloud). 

 

Soft music from the living room blended with the faint squeaky toy Nicky was chewing on filled in the silence. Rio didn’t look at Wanda. She couldn’t stand to see the face of,

You know I’m right. 

 

And yet even through her frustration- Rio was content on being there. Sitting across from her closest friend, not drowning in her worries alone. Wanda may be annoying when she was right, but she was still such a calming presence. One who confronted you while comforting you at the same time. Sometimes Rio thought about how she was genuinely too pure for the world. 

 

“I think she’s busy more than anything. That’s my vote” Wanda said. “Or..maybe she’s feeling the same as you were this morning”

 

“Which is my fault for starting it”

 

“No, not necessarily” She shrugged. 

 

Wanda took a sigh, propping her chin on her palm with soft eyes that spoke gentle unspoken words. How everything would be fine and work out for the best. Even if Rio couldn’t see it. 

 

“You two figured out how to not hate each other..” She pointed out. “I think this will be easier than that”

 

Rio bit on her bottom lip, looking down as her knee started to bounce. She never even had to utter the question aloud for an answer. Wanda just spoke as if she heard the words in her mind. 

 

“And if it isn’t easy? You’ll both find your way through. I know it” 

 

Wanda snickered, kicking her from under the table right after with a quick, “Remember, I was the one years ago who said Agatha might be more”

“Of a pain in my ass?” Rio looked up. “Yeah, just a bit”

 

Wanda smiled, thankful Rio was finding her humor somewhat. 

 

“Hate to be the bearer of bad news, sweetie but..sounds like you were the pain in the ass first on this”

 

“You know, you could just be on my side without the calling out bullshit”

 

“I wouldn’t ever be your friend if I did that. We both know it”

 

Rio didn't get a chance to reply. Wanda had kicked her again, picking up the towel to lightly snap her arm with before jumping out of her seat. 

 

“Now! Since you came over, it is happy cleaning-”

 

“No!” Rio groaned like a child. “I came over to be sad! Not clean!” 

 

Wanda spun around to find Rio a towel to help dry dishes off with, singing over her words a loud, 

 

“We will clean, and dance! Then you shall call Agatha and reconfess your sins and love-”

 

“What sins?!” Rio couldn’t help but subtly smile over the woman’s antics. “If anyone has them it’s you for making your depressed friend fucking clean”

 

Wanda tossed the towel at her while handing her a few plates right after. She ignored her completely, counting down the list of things that needed to be dusted and vacuumed- giving her the entire schedule of the day ahead. 

 

Rio wanted to be mad, annoyed, walk out in a fit of rage. But all she could do was grab a plate and towel, not offer an argument. Only snarky comments while silently being thankful for the distraction. 

 

Maybe later that night when she was alone again. When the thoughts, worries and regrets all boiled up and over her- She’d call. 

 

What was the worst that could happen? Agatha wouldn’t answer? She wasn’t doing that to begin with. That was the main root of the problem besides Rio regretting how their morning after was spent. 

 

Though before she could ocmpoletely focus in on the hectic cleaning day Wanda had planned- Rio pulled out her phone to send one little message. 

 

“She answer?” Wanda asked.

 

Rio typed the few words, hoping for a reply to know Agatha was at least safe and not tossed off a mountain. That’d be common courtesy to say that at least, no? 

 

“Uh..” Rio stammered, biting on her lips as she stared at the screen. 

 

For a woman who wasn’t religious, she silently prayed for the typing bubble to appear. However, it didn’t. She locked her phone after a few seconds, dropping it with a shake of her head. 

 

“Give it time” Wanda said. “She stared at you like an addict. Her withdraws will take over soon enough”

Rio snickered as she dried the second plate, stacking it on top of the other. “Comparing her to a drug addict now?”

 

“For you?” Wanda laughed. “Like I said, we were very amused with how she looked at you. Wondered if she was going to pin you on the table right then and ther-”

 

“Oh, you’re just..wrong. Gross. Bye”

 

“Don’t give me the innocent act!” Wanda exclaimed with a smile. “Listen, you may have been a top with other girls. I know that. But that woman has you whip-”

 

Rio dropped the plate, looking up with offense as she scoffed, “Are you calling me a bottom right now?”

 

Wanda shrugged. “If the shoe fits-”

 

“I am not!” She exclaimed, cheeks burning as she shivered over the memory of Agatha. “I- No, I-”

 

“Agatha topping a top,” Wanda snickered. “Makes so much sense. Adorable she has that power over you, really”

 

“Again, I came here to feel better. Not be accused of such things” 

 

“Mhm,” Wanda hummed. “Dry those plates- Or do you only let Agatha tell you what to do?”

 

Rio shook her head. “I hate it here” She muttered. 

 

Wanda snickered. “I know”

 

 

 

It was creeping up to midnight when Agatha finally checked her phone. She had been ignoring it since Billy showed up all giddy and excited for their roadtrip. The woman tried telling herself for once she was focusing on the present, living in the moment and enjoying a tiny vacation from her normal. 

 

When in reality…it was Rio. Just. Rio. 

 

Agatha briefly saw the first message when it came through. Her eyes skimmed it before her finger locked the phone in a panic, dropping it into her purse to be forgotten about for the day. Though when they stopped at their final rest area (They had spent the day sight seeing and shopping on their way there) and Billy was taking too long in the bathroom- Curiosity had gotten the best of her.

 

The first text lifted her heart a bit. It wasn’t long after Rio had bolted out of her room, leaving her alone in a heavy silence. Agatha read those words over and over. Rio missed her. She wouldn’t lie about that..right?

 

The following three lifted her heart before it smashed to the ground below. Rio clearly had been thinking about her, worried for her safety and wanted updates during the trip. As much as it made her feel warm for a moment, it also somewhat destroyed her at the same time. 

 

Agatha had dated women in the past, but for some reason they were never, well… this. Some confessed love, sure. And maybe at the time Agatha thought their definition of love made sense. However, Rio’s weighed heavier, meant something else to her. 

 

Even after a tense morning, Rio was checking in. While even on the best of terms with her exes, none of them ever cared when she left for a couple days. The only messages she ever got was goodbye’s and asking when she’d be back. And here was Rio sending multiple messages almost begging to hear from her. 

 

Agatha should love this. She should be relieved and happy to see Rio wasn’t running from her. The woman waited for the feeling to come back. How she adored Rio, wanted to only talk to her and be thankful her packing early didn’t scare her off. 

 

I don’t deserve her. 

This is too much. 

What am I even doing? 

I’ll just hurt her in the long run. 

 

The thoughts were aggressive, brutal. Agatha Harkness may come off as someone confident beyond words. An ego that skyrocketed so high out of the universe’s atmosphere. When in reality, she was a product of a mother who hated her. A woman who spent her childhood hiding in closets from kids at school, listening to cruel words and accusations people held against her. 

 

She had worked tirelessly throughout her adult life to either ignore or grow from what she knew. Some days were better than others, but maybe her past relationships felt easier because she didn’t care as much as she thought she did. Maybe it was choosing women who didn’t care. Who only liked her for the sex and good time. 

 

While Rio didn’t see her for just that. No. They started off as enemies, Rio never wanting anything to do with her. If it was just sex, it’d only be that. They’d have zero connection. Rio wouldn’t be smiling up at her like a fool as Agatha rambled about nothing. She wouldn’t be texting her with care for how she was, if they were safe. 

 

And Agatha wouldn’t be staring at her phone like someone was holding her at gunpoint. 

 

Slowly she realized how hard she had fallen. Sure, Rio was someone she knew she fell hopelessly for the last few years. She had a stupid little crush. So she thought, anyway. Sometimes Agatha acknowledged how it grew into something more, but always chalked it up to the unknown. Part of her figured once she experienced Rio, it wouldn’t be the same. 


To be fair, she was partially right. This wasn’t the same. Just not in the way she thought. 

 

Everything was intensified. Agatha couldn’t think about the rest of her life without Rio tagging along. She felt overwhelmed experiencing what love was for the first time. Something she thought she knew, but held no knowledge about. And honestly?  

 

Love terrified the fucking shit out of her. Especially after that morning they had. 

 

When she left Rio’s the day before, it hurt. Sure. The thought Rio didn’t view her the same way sucked. However, it wasn’t the same. She admitted to being loved, allowed someone to say it to her without letting it be a thought that passed through one ear out the other. Agatha put herself in such a vulnerable state only to experience a piece of what it was to be ripped from it. 

 

Maybe Agatha couldn’t handle the risk of hurting that bad. The idea of giving that pain to Rio either? She should stop them while they were ahead, save them both from such horror. 

 

“Ready?” 

 

Billy’s voice snapped her awake from the trance of being stuck in Rio’s texts. She locked her phone, dropped it back in her purse with a nod. 

 

“You’re driving” She pointed while opening the passenger’s side. 

 

He didn’t argue, eager to complete their trip so they could both crash into bed. The sight seeing, shopping, all of it was worth it. Both had forgotten though how exhausting a trip through the mountains could be. Especially when Agatha had to distract Billy from a panic attack when they passed through where his accident was. 

 

As he adjusted the seat and mirrors, starting the car and putting the gear in drive- Agatha took his phone to set up music, not bothering to look at her’s anymore. She couldn’t handle doing so. The thought of Rio texting again or her accidentally sending something back- 

 

Fuck. 

 

Billy merged out on the highway. One that was busy hours prior now quiet in the dead of night. She turned the radio up just enough to sit in the background. Wicked Game by Chris Isaak. 

 

Course. This shit is in his playlist. 

Fine. It was a good song, whatever. But Agatha tried to ignore the lyrics the best she could. How falling in love, this world would only break your heart, ya-deeya-dee-ya-da . 

 

Agatha closed her eyes, elbow on the windowsill as she pinched the bridge of her nose. 

 

This kept happening. Songs, videos, shows and movies- Everything reminded her of Rio. It had somewhat prior to them getting together, but accelerated into full drive once they went from enemies to lovers. 

 

The second Rio sat in her passenger seat, Agatha’s world became Rio coded. She couldn’t escape it no matter how hard she tried, far she traveled, any of it. 

 

Though as Billy settled into the middle lane, comfortable with the speed of sixty mph- Agatha always flew at eighty or ninety, but whatever. She wished it was only the music that reminded her of Rio. 

 

“So..” Billy started, fingertips drumming on the steering wheel. “Can I ask you something?”

 

No.

 

“You just did” 

 

He rolled his eyes, ignoring her sarcastic answer. He had become extremely accustomed to them to the point the words barely touched or scared him like they used to. 

 

“You and Professor Vidal..”

 

Oh, double no. Fuck to the no. No, no, no, no! 

 

Agatha’s heart dropped, breath stuck in her chest as all her limbs tensed as if poison turned her blood into stone. She didn’t look over, tried to settle the fear in her tone as she replied,

 

“What about her?” 

 

Billy was blind to the woman beside him. Even if they were in the daylight with the sun blasting rays down on her- He wouldn’t see the sudden discomfort, fear, she wore. 

 

“She called me last night, uh- Demanding for your address, actually” He confessed as if Agatha didn’t know. “Is all alright or..”

 

No. It isn’t. Or, maybe it is. I don’t know. 

 

Wasn’t torturing herself earlier in the parking lot with these thoughts enough? Did the universe hate her that much to make her revisit this so soon? Especially trapped in a car with a notorious kid who held a record of never knowing when to shut the hell up?

 

“Agatha?”

 

“Just,” She sighed, hand up as she closed her eyes. “Mind your business on this one, alright?” 

 

He didn’t respond for a second. Agatha thought for a blissful moment her voice scared him. She was typically rough, sarcastic. But even she couldn’t deny how the soft, quiet, weak and tender voice sounded more frightening. 

 

Of course though, in Billy fashion, he couldn’t shut his mouth for the life of him.

 

“No, sorry- Agatha. I can’t-”

 

“You can, you’re just choosing not to” Agatha argued.

 

“Not after you’ve helped me with everything, no” He laughed with a shake of his head. “You talk to me about anything and I want to do the same! I know, I’m still a kid in your eyes, but-”

 

“Exactly. Kid in my eyes so shut the hell up about this”

 

“What is it about her?” He ignored her completely, glancing over before switching his eyes back on the road. “You two have been…different. I-”

 

“She’s an asshole” Agatha said. “Point blank. Clear as day. No other explanation. 

 

He scoffed. “No. Not true. Yes, she’s..scary, maybe- But..very kind!”

 

“Oh, is she?” Agatha snickered. 

 

“Yes” He nodded. “She helps me even when I don’t ask. That stupid copier, for example? It’s like she can sense when I’m about to lose it when it won’t work” He chuckled. “She’s a hero for that thing and so much more” 

 

“Course she is..” Agatha muttered, slouching in her seat more while hiding half of her face. “Is that all? Or do you want to keep preaching about Bitch Vidal?”

 

“No. I want to know what happened with you two” He said. “I don’t- Actually, never have understood the sworn enemies thing between you two. She has the same sense of humor as you-”

 

“How do you even know she has humor?” She asked as if she didn’t know herself. 

 

“Like I said, she does help me out. She’s scary, but..still cracks some good jokes. Like you! Like uh, teasing and insulty and-”

 

“Annoying” Agatha ended. “Change of subject and stop looking at me. Keep your eyes on the road”

 

“What about-”

 

“William” 

 

“Okay hey- No full name basis is needed” He pointed with an eyeroll. “I am just trying to be a good friend”

 

“Who says I want you to be?”

 

He scoffed. “You’re on a road trip with me, Agatha. We’re friends. Besties even-”

 

“Ew, do not use that word” She cringed. 

 

“Oh my god” He rolled his eyes. “You get so defensive about her”

 

“I don’t talk to you about anything” She argued.

 

He scoffed. “We just gossiped about Jen and Alice’s relationship, Lilia’s secret affair with God knows who. Every fling and relationship I’ve had down to stories about your mother, but you’re REALLY going to try and tell me we don’t talk?!”

 

“Exactly. About other things, peopl-”

 

“Rio is people”

 

“Oo, look at you. So grown. Using her actual first name!” She teased, dropping back in her seat with a muttered, “Just shut it”

 

“Oh would you stop avoiding it?!” He laughed.

 

Agatha looked back out the window, debating jumping out of the moving vehicle all together. Who cared if she died from injuries or the tractor trailer behind them ran her over. It’d save her from this at least. 

 

“Why did she need your address?”

 

“To leave a bag of flaming shit on my doorstep” Agatha snapped, looking back at him with disgust in her eyes. “She’s a wicked human being” 

 

Wicked for making me fall in love, really.

 

“Yeah, no” He laughed. “You would have made me throw that out for you and would have called the second it happened” 

 

“I was sparing you for once” 

 

“You aren’t sparing me by leaving me in the dark like this, you know?” He pointed out. “She’s never really talked to me. Didn’t even have my number, I don’t think. What was so important for her to see you, Agatha?”

 

Relentless little shit. 

 

Whatever. 

 

Fine. 

 

Maybe..she could talk about it. Somewhat, really. Not like she had to go into full blown details of how she had fallen in love for years with a woman who hadn’t even spared her a passing glance until recently. 

 

Well, no- She was always amused catching Rio’s gaze from across the room. It was different now though. No glare, no storming out of the room followed. She stayed put. Instead of running, Rio usually fell into her arms or pulled her closer. 

 

She could shut down the conversation at any given moment. Jump out of the car, threaten his life, etc. Agatha knew too if she gave him a sliver of an answer, he may shut up for awhile until curiosity really took the best of him again. 

 

Agatha took in a breath, drumming her fingertips rhythmically on the tip of her thumb. 

 

“We uh,” She stammered, slightly shrugging. “ Lately...we hang ou-”

 

Just as she was about to open up, tell someone else besides the mirror and Rio how she felt. Blue and red lights lit up behind them, a siren echoed on their tail. She jumped up to spin around, finding the cop car catching up to him. Her eyes then flickered to see the sixty mph went up to eighty five. A slow grin crawled on her face, amusement covering her head to toe. 

 

"Oh no.." Billy said. “Oh, no! No! I- I-”

 

“Just pull over, kid” Agatha snorted. “You’ll be fine. Just a speeding ticket-”

 

“You speed all the time! I accidentally did so and I get pulled over?!” He yelled. 

 

The car drifted off to the right slowly. Agatha was trying to control her laughter over the situation. 

 

“So much for your bragging of never getting pulled over in your few short years of driving” She mused. 

 

Billy put the car in park as Agatha opened the dashboards for the registration. As entertaining as this was, Agatha knew she’d have to help him get through this. The kid was filled with anxiety over the smallest things. This was probably worse than him nearly dying off a mountain. 

 

“Roll down the window” She said. 

 

“Right, right” He nodded, bones shaking so hard Agatha swore she heard them rattling. “Ag-”

 

“Honey, you’ll be fine” She softly assured, reaching over to squeeze his shoulder for a little reassurance. “This is fun, but-”

 

“It is not fun!” He exclaimed. “What if I get arrested?!”

 

“Do you have a warrant out or a violent history you’ve never told me about?”

 

“Not that I know of!”

 

“Oh my god,” Agatha laughed. “I think you’d know-”

 

“I-”

 

“Hey there,” The officer appeared. She gave a stern smile, Billy whipped around as he choked on his words. “You know why I pulled you over tonight?”

 

“Uh, I- I-”

 

“You were speeding” Agatha muttered. 

 

“Speeding!” He said. “Yes! Too fast, I’m so sorry. I’ll never do that again. I don’t even like Nascar!” 

 

Nascar? The fuck is he on about?

 

Agatha snorted, hand covering her mouth to stifle her laugh as she reached for her phone. Just as she swiped the screen, her messages with Rio appeared. The place her instinct was telling her to go. Right then, it hit her like a gunshot straight through her. A violent punch that broke her heart. 

 

She wanted to text Rio, tell her the situation and how he just spewed Nascar for some reason. But, her fear of falling in love, allowing herself to be hurt took over. She dropped her phone back in the purse, looking over to find Billy nearly losing his wallet. 

 

“Can I just take out his license and mine for you?” Agatha leaned over. 

 

The officer chuckled with a nod. “If he’s okay with that, sure. My first time being pulled over made me a wreck as well”

 

Agatha snickered, slapping his chest with the back of her hand before taking his wallet. “He isn’t sure if he has a criminal history so..you may want to check that”

 

“Wha- NO! No, she’s kidding, I-”

 

Agatha handed her their ID’s, sitting back as the officer told them to hang tight. They sat in silence for a few seconds before Billy broke. 

 

“..I’m not forgetting you just told me you’re hanging out with Professor Vidal. Even if I might go to jail now”

 

If it wasn’t for the last comment, Agatha would have gotten out of the car and asked the officer for a ride to get away from him. However, she just rolled her eyes, shaking her head. 

 

“You continue to say her name and I will make sure you’re arrested. How’s that?”

 

He gasped, eyes wide with his jaw dropped. “Not even funny, Agatha”

 

“Oh, actually all of this right now is funny” She smiled. “This is the best road trip of my life”

 

“I’m going to kill you”

 

“...Officer!” Agatha turned as she raised her voice. “He threatened-”

 

“Agatha!” He jumped over to cover her mouth.

 

The two started to shove each other, half wrestling the best they could while buckled in their seats. Agatha tried to not laugh, but..it was hard not to. Even if the thought of talking about Rio was daunting, she hated how it still felt nice that someone else had a little smidge of knowledge about them. 


And plus, Billy being pulled over for the first time? That was worth the conversation that barely lasted five minutes. 

 

“I’m going to get to the bottom of this” He warned. 

 

“Not when you’re rotting in a jail cell. Oh! Maybe you’ll find a boyfriend if you drop the soap-”

 

“That isn’t funny!”

 

She fell into a fit of laughter, distracted by bullying and teasing him completely. Only later on when they got to his brother’s would she look at her phone to find three missed calls on top of the prior texts.

 

And maybe then…Agatha would allow herself to reply. 



The "Bullshit" Tale of Agatha Cares

Agatha gasped as the cold water splashed her face, freezing her skin for a few short seconds. She held the sink, listened as the water flowed, admired the sun’s glow on the white marble before her. And for those few moments, barely enough to last a full minute…she didn’t think about her. 

 

Then like a punch, reality reminded her she wasn’t safe from her thoughts..

 

Rio.

 

Her hand aggressively jerked the water off, snatching the towel to cover her face. She wished the fabric could dry off and wipe away Rio Vidal. Wash her completely, get rid of the woman who drove her mad. 

 

If it were that easy, Agatha would have invested in all the towels in the world years ago. 

 

Surprisingly (typically traveling took a major toll on her) Agatha hadn't slept. She may have gotten an hour or two, but definitely not enough to be a functional human being. Which didn't work out in her favor. 

 

By the following morning, Billy was giddy to meet his brother at the diner for brunch. The start of an amazing trip for him. The start of way too much socializing for Agatha's liking. 

 

Billy better count his blessings Agatha had a soft spot for him. Even if she wasn’t struggling with what she left at home, socializing was still her worst nightmare.  

 

She had Billy take off to the diner without her that morning. It was only two blocks away from the apartment they were staying at. Tommy had a few roommates, leaving it too crowded for them to crash there. Agatha would have argued for their own place regardless. Airbnb was a blessing for introverts like herself. 

 

Slowly, Agatha crawled out of bed and forced herself to take a quick shower. She hadn't dared to look at her phone. Not until she had to. Agatha wasn't sure if she could stomach seeing Rio's texts again. 

 

I'm horrible. 

An asshole. 

Why can't I just reply? 

 

She was a fucking adult for crying outloud too busy hiding like some immature teenager. Hell, Billy would have probably handled the situation better. And yet, Agatha couldn't get herself to fix it. She struggled with facing her fears, sinking into who she worked so hard to stray away from. 

 

Old habits die hard, the saying goes. And Agatha hated that she was the definition of that. 

 

Eventually, Agatha was forced to look at her phone. Not only to let Billy know she wasn't dead and was still on her way. But also? 

 

Agatha canceled her classes for Monday and Tuesday. 

 

The two would be back by Monday morning, but Agatha couldn't imagine walking in the building. She briefly debated quitting her job completely, but that wasn't possible. 

 

And she had to be a mature adult somewhat, after all…right? 

 

Ultimately, Agatha forced herself to stay away from Rio's messages. She had muted her, deleted their chat before ever opening it. Her thumb swiped away the notifications of missed calls and two voicemails. 

 

She couldn't do it. 

She couldn't face her. 

 

Such a coward. 

 

Agatha took a deep breath when she approached the front doors of the diner. A mini rundown building that had definitely seen better days. Sooner she went in, the sooner this would all be over and the next few days would go by quick..was that a good thing though? Agatha didn’t want to know. 

 

Billy had told her they were in the back. A bigger table to fit Tommy’s and Billy’s old, new, friends. 

 

Fucking yay. 

 

Hanging out with twenty something year olds was not in Agatha’s mind. Originally, this was only supposed to be a trip to see his brother. And now? 

 

“Sure! Get the whole gang together, why not?” Agatha muttered to herself as she spotted the table. 

 

Billy spotted her instantly, jumping up with a bright smile. 

 

“Agatha!” 

 

He rushed over, gesturing to her with way too much excitement (Shocking, truly). 

 

“Everyone,” He smiled. “I’d like you to meet a very important role model in my life”

 

Deep down beneath everything else going on in her mind, Agatha’s heart did melt a bit. He was sweet. She loved being seen as a guidance, some kind of teacher to him. For a woman who grew up being told to shut up and ignored constantly, it was a surprise. A nice one too. 

 

Tommy grinned. “So you're the legend in my brother's stories?” 

 

Agatha scoffed. “Legend? More like his worst nightmare” 

 

The rest chuckled in response. Billy gestured down the table to the open seat right next to-

 

“You’re next to my cousin,” He said, leading the way to pull the chair out for her. “Kate, this is Agatha. Agatha, Kate!”

 

Kate was not in her twenties. Not by a long shot. Agatha roughly would estimate she was exactly her age or a year, maybe two, younger- Possibly older. 

 

The woman Billy was gesturing to looked kind, soft. She was bringing the mimosa up to her lips when their eyes met. The blonde hair made the blue eyes pop in the warm sunlight shining through. She lowered the drink, wiping off her lips with a tiny wave. 

 

Agatha side glanced at Billy who looked nervous, fiddling with his fingers and chewing on his bottom lip and- Shit. Agatha clicked it without a second to waste.

 

He’d briefly talked about trying to set Agatha up on a date. She shut him down left and right. Especially lately with Rio being the only woman she ever wanted. And now? 

 

Shit. 

Rio can't find out about this. 

 

She forced a smile. One that made Billy step back and see through the facade. His lips parted to speak, but his brother called him back over and he took the chance to flee. 

 

Agatha sighed, sitting in the vacant space next to her.

 

Kate snickered. “We’ve been set up..haven’t we?”

 

She scoffed in reply, shaking her head while sending subtle daggers down the table. 

 

“Bunch of twenty something fuckin’ year olds. You surprised? I’m not” 

 

The woman chuckled, raising her glass in the air with a small, 

“To being conned” 

 

Agatha hummed, looking around for the waiter to order a drink. 

 

“It’s good you joined him though. We appreciate it” Kate said. “My cousin can..well-”

 

“Be a dumbass?” 

 

“In a kind way” Kate said. 

 

Agatha smirked. “We did get pulled over on the way here. Has he confessed to that yet?” 

 

Kate shot up in her chair, eyes wide with a strong laugh that made the other’s heads turn. Her jaw dropped, leaning closer to Agatha as she whispered,

 

“Was he driv-”

 

“Yep,” Agatha popped the ‘p’ with a slow nod, eyes closed as she listened to Kate break down laughing. “Poor kid nearly shit himself right there”

 

“Oh my god” Kate laughed, wiping tears as she leaned back to catch her breath. “Oh..I’m so giving him shit for that later. He got a ticket too?”

 

“The whole package” 

 

“This is beautiful. Suddenly agreeing to be here isn’t so bad” She snickered.
