“Can’t agree?” Kate asked.

 

Agatha looked back over, taking a second before puffing out a small laugh. 

 

“Not really, no”

 

“Wanna’ talk about it?”

 

Agatha laughed, but Kate didn’t let her reply. 

 

“We will most likely never see each other again. I’m not looking to date, clearly you have another woman on your mind and-”

 

“What?” Agatha’s voice cracked, clearing her throat with a forced chuckle. “Why would I have a woman on my mind? Huh?”

 

“Because we are both grown women who know the look of heartache. It doesn’t look good on you. Your eyes are dark and-”

 

“Wow” Agatha scoffed. “You have some fucking nerve” She muttered. 

 

Kate shrugged, sipping from the drink before replying. 

 

“You’re the only woman my age here. Give me something. If I hear about some TikTok trend again or what’s going on Twitter- I’m going to lose my fucking mind” 

 

She smirked, a little laugh with a nod. “Yeah, I never understand when Billy goes on about that. None of us at work do, to be fair” 

 

“Exactly” She nodded. “So..talk-”

 

“No, I-”

 

“Girlfriend? Boyfrie-”

 

“Ew, no”

 

“But you didn’t cringe at the first one, so! This is a girlfriend”

 

Agatha took in a deep breath, wondering softly to herself if Rio was still her girlfriend. What would she be going back to if she never replied to her? Was she running out of time? Agatha didn’t want to think about it. Even if it was all she could think about. 

 

“Why did Billy set you up if-”

 

“Complicated”

 

“Hidden? Closeted? Sworn enemies or-”

 

“You ask a lot of fucking questions, Kate” Agatha scoffed. 

 

“You are not fun, Agatha” She snickered. “Okay- If it makes you feel better..” She held the nearly empty glass up. “This is my third..maybe fourth one”

 

Agatha’s eyes widened. “You’ve only been here for like an hour or two”

 

“Yeah. My cousins and all their little friends. Again, give me something here” She said. “Don’t make a woman beg”

 

Fuck. 

 

Agatha hated what that did to her. The memory screamed, ran through, shook her mind of Rio begging for her. Not just to cum, but even at her apartment door. The love confession wasn’t a beg, but a plea to hear her. 

 

And I’m losing her..

 

“Plea-”

 

“Will it make you shut the fuck up?”

 

“I’ll even buy you as many mimosas as you’d like! They’re wonderful here”

 

Agatha snorted. “I can tell..” 

 

She took in a deep breath, thankful for the waiter coming over and Kate ordering her a drink. It’d definitely make discussing the topic of Rio easier. Thinking about her as well wouldn’t hurt so much. 

 

“Why are you hidden?” 

 

“What do you mean?”

 

“Like,” She swallowed down the rest of her drink with a wave of her hand, gesturing for Agatha to wait. “Why doesn’t my cousin know you have a girlfriend?”

 

Do I have one?

 

“Complicated”

 

“Aren’t all relationships that?” 

 

The waiter placed the mimosa down before her. Agatha almost snatched it out of his hand with how quick she moved for it. 

 

She downed the sweet liquid almost all in one go. Her eyes shut, lips pulled back to lick the remaining taste off. 

 

“Drink in hand, mimosa working it’s magic-”

 

“Not yet”

 

“Still!” Kate laughed. “Talk” 

 

“God..” She muttered, shaking her head. “Really uh..it doesn’t matter” 

 

It did matter, that was the problem. Agatha knew she was doomed even deeper when there was an urge kicking her to talk. 

 

To a stranger, nonetheless. 

 

For a woman who never opened up, barely showed a crack in her armor- Rio had done damage. She was breaking her not only for herself, but for the rest of the world to see. 

 

Agatha was crumbling, falling apart, and it was all Rio Vidal's fault. 

 

“I can see it in your eyes..” Kate sang. 

 

Agatha scoffed. “Fucking creep-”

 

“Why aren't you answering her?” 

 

Agatha took in a deep breath, keeping her head down as the question circled like a pack of crows in her mind. All she had to do was answer. That was it. Logically it was becoming more obvious Rio wanted to fix things (So Agatha hoped, anyway). 

 

And yet-

 

“Agatha..” Kate said. “This isn't fair to do this to her and I don't even know the poor girl”

 

“She's the one that left like that. You have no idea what you’re on about and like I said- Have quite a bit of fucking nerve trying”

 

“See, this is why you need to talk” Kate chuckled. “I don't even know how she left and you're quick to be so defensive on it!” 

 

“Because..” Agatha shrugged. “It's..complicated” 

 

“Is it?” 

 

No. 

Yes. 

Maybe? 

 

Agatha was complicated. That was more the truth than anything else. 

 

“Do you not want to fix things?” 

 

“How do you know there's anything able to be fixed?” 

 

“Because if there wasn't..you wouldn't be so shut down, defensive, and clearly stuck in thought over her” 

 

Shit. 

 

Agatha sat back, avoiding eye contact with the woman who was nailing her with ease. Not the way Agatha liked her women nailing her either. 

 

Well…no more women, just a woman.  

 

She wasn’t used to a woman, another person, putting up such a battle. Agatha usually scared them off, but she couldn’t even find the strength to create witty insults or toss a drink in the woman’s face. 

 

This was all Rio’s fault. Wait, would that work?

 

Maybe Agatha could find anger and blame easier with Rio than anything else. Rio wasn’t good for her, right? She was turning Agatha into something she wasn’t. 

 

Her entire life was built to be a confident, independent, strong woman. Someone who didn’t let another take her down. She swore to herself after growing up with her mother, no one would make her that vulnerable ever again and-

 

“You’re scared” 

 

Agatha froze, her body tense as she repeated the words in her mind. 

 

Did she wear the emotion on her sleeve now? Was it not something she could hide any longer? 

 

“I-”

 

“You know what..” 

 

Agatha laughed, pulling out cash to put on the table. She didn’t know how much the drink cost, but it didn’t matter to her. A twenty would surely cover her small part of the bill. And when Billy asked why she left, a migraine would be her reply. 

 

“I’m gonna’ head back. It was lovely meeting you, Kate”

 

The woman sighed, shaking her head. “Honey, I didn’t mean to-”

 

“Don’t call me that” She pointed.

 

Agatha nodded to Billy who read her eyes. He gave a sympathetic smile with a nod of his own, mouthing the words, 

 

“It’s okay” 

 

The woman collected her belongings, saying soft goodbyes and promised to see them all later on. She knew Billy had her back. That was one thing she adored about that kid. He was supportive, protective, and looked out for her in his own way. 

 

She stepped out onto the sidewalk, taking in a deep breath while looking around at the people walking by. Just when she thought her life couldn’t get any worse?

 

Every brunette was Rio. 

Every shade of green was Rio. 

Every tree, every plant in her sight-

 

Everything in her life now was Rio. 

 

She was miles away and had hoped this trip would temporarily make her forget, but that was impossible. 

 

Agatha couldn’t slip into her old ways. She was changed for the rest of her life. Rio was screaming in her mind, heart, every piece of her. While Agatha had been crushing on her for a few years now, it was never this. 

 

The woman placed a hand over her heart, the other firmly gripping her hip as if that’d keep her on the ground. Heavy breaths, chaotic mind, and a destructive decision joined the mix. 

 

Agatha pulled her phone out, fingers trembling as she found the voicemail app. The most recent two belonged to Rio. She had been deadset on never listening, but like an addict who couldn’t stand the withdrawal- 

 

She hit play. 

 

The woman brought the phone up to her ear, forcing herself to walk down towards the Airbnb. She knew after listening, hiding under the covers or maybe drowning herself would be the only options available. 

 

There was a breath on the phone, maybe a soft cry? Agatha couldn’t tell. It didn’t last long before a small, 

 

“Hey..” Rio whispered, clearing her throat right after. “I uh- God, I’m a psycho. I don’t even know how many times I’ve texted you by now”

 

She laughed, but it wasn’t one that was filled with humor. The sound was pathetic, wet with tears and soft sobs that were being suffocated to make it through the call.  

 

“If you get a restraining order, I’d understand but uh..” She said. “I hate how we left that- How I left that. You..well- No. Sorry, fuck”

 

Rio fumbled with the phone, Agatha could nearly envision how that looked. She was probably adorable even while looking like a trainwreck. 

 

“Just..sorry” 

 

The voicemail ended and Agatha was shivering like the air had turned into a blizzard temperature. She looked around, disorientated but coherent enough to know the area. A few more minutes, she’d be hiding in the apartment from the world. 

 

And yet? She couldn’t hold off to press play on the second one. 

 

“Okay!” Rio laughed. “This time- I got it. Yep!” 

 

Is she..drunk? Agatha couldn’t blame her if she was. 

 

“We fucked up” She said. “It takes two to tango and I walked out and YOUUU are being an asshole by ignoring me!” 

 

Okay. She’s not wrong there. 

 

“So! That being said,” Rio took a moment. Agatha could hear the clink of the beer bottle in the background. “We have a few options. Fuck through it, ignore this ever happened, or I track you down and hold you hostage till you’re mine again!”

 

Agatha couldn’t hold back the hint of a smile on her face. She imagined in front of her how Rio’s drunken body swayed side to side. How her lips were pursed in a pouting smile. The little look she gave Agatha when the liquor was too much and all she wanted to do was snuggle in her side. 

 

“So uh..choose!” Rio demanded. “No matter the choice- I love you, you love me and I could start singing fucking Barney right now- My little cousin lived on that shit, Agatha. Ugh. You would have lost your mind and…uh…fuck, that’s-”

 

The woman snickered softly to herself as she listened. Rio was always so chaotic. Sometimes even sober her rambles were scattered into multiple different topics across the board. Drunk Rio only accelerated that. 

 

“I’m literally talking about a show, fake purple ass dinosaur for toddlers…but I love dinosaurs…have I told you that? No! No, shit. I hid my boxers with that print because you’d laugh and..” 

 

I love her. Oh my god. Agatha repeated to herself. 

 

She loved how stupid the woman was. How she overthought things like a maniac to the point she hid a pair of boxers. The way she came off to others as a mature, serious, boring adult in her career and home life. Only to be a humorous, sweet, kind soul that adored things no one would guess.

 

Agatha knew she loved her Lego sets. Some sat on the wall of her office. Rio tried to brush it off saying it was a gift, but Agatha saw the stacked untouched boxes in the closet. 

 

Rio watched cartoons every Saturday morning, telling Agatha that Nicky adored them and that’s why she put them on. 

 

She also loved stupid Dad jokes, Spiderman movies, everything no one would guess and-

 

Does she really think that’s all stupid? 

 

Agatha never made fun of her for any of it. She enjoyed the same things, even wanted them to have a date where they just colored and watched movies. 

 

Did Rio not realize it was a reason Agatha fell in love so hard? She learned an entirely different side of Rio than Professor Vidal ever showed. 

 

“Maybe this is why you’re ignoring me..” Rio whispered. “I ran off..immature as fuck, I guess and..” She sniffled, taking a breath before adding, “Do you regret me, Agatha?”

 

“Never” Agatha whispered as if Rio was on the other line and not just a voicemail. 

 

“I regret walking out- Running, really..the way I did, but..” Rio sighed. “I miss you. Do you miss me? Fuck. What am I doing? Okay uh..I’m gonna..”

 

Agatha bit on her cheek, almost hard enough to draw blood from it. She waited for the end, wondering what Rio had to say, but then..

 

Silence. 

 

She looked at the screen, seeing the voicemail ended and was ready to replay if she wanted it to. Agatha stopped walking, not caring if it was in the middle of the busy sidewalk. Her heart was on the pavement beneath her feet. She was stuck, unable to figure out what was next. 

 

Call her. 

 

It wasn’t that simple- It is. 

 

Agatha was changed for the rest of her life. Never again would she be able to hide her emotions, focus on other women, act as if she didn’t have a heartbreak destroying her from within. 

 

Unfortunately though? It wasn’t that easy to face who she now was. Reaching out to Rio felt too soon, not enough time to accept the love she had was taking over her entire life. While some would argue if the love was strong enough, Agatha could face everything head on and be blind to all else. 

 

But..Agatha Harkness was still not people. She never would be. The woman created the definition of complicated, difficult, all of the above. 

 

She’d find Rio. 

She’d apologize profusely, make it up to her, buy her all the dinosaur boxers and everything she ever wanted. 

 

Agatha already started to rehearse what she’d say when she saw her. 

 

“You’re stupid for thinking those things would make me love you less”

“I’m stupid for never replying and taking this long” 

“You’ll never understand what you’ve done to me”

“I’m in pieces for you”

“I’ll spend eternity doing anything you want”

 

She just needed some extra time. Just a few more days. Some time to process, accept, figure out how she would function not being who she once was. 

 

The only thing Agatha wasn’t thinking about? Selfishly the woman wasn’t considering what Rio was going through. 

 

She was so stuck in her mind, terrible worry over how to cope with losing her armor. The wall she had stacked so high only to be blown to pieces, dismantled to bits within a short amount of time. There was no thought to how Rio could possibly not want to repair them if Agatha kept ignoring her. 

 

Maybe part of that as well was Agatha not wanting to face she was hurting Rio by doing this. She was changed, but still had parts of herself ruled by an egocentric mind. One she’d have to also let go of moving forward if she wanted to be loved. 

 

In her mind, things could be fixed. Agatha Harkness always got what she wanted through demands, power and striking fear through others. 

 

However, love was new territory. Especially one that was ripping her apart, turning her into someone she had never been. 

 

Agatha had a lot to learn, so much to accept and change about herself. 

 

And yet? She’s worth it. She’s so fucking worth it. 

 

Agatha was camped out on the couch later that night. A fleece blanket covering her, one of Rio’s hoodies snug against her arms and chest. The hood draped over her head, partially hiding her face from the rest of the world. Well, mainly an empty apartment until the front door opened and shut close to eleven that night. 

 

Billy hummed as he walked through the dining room, glancing to where the TV in the living room played, finding Agatha hidden in her own cave. 

 

He gave a sad smile, rummaging through the bag to find the container of leftover fries. It was something he always did. Especially when he noticed Agatha was having a bad day in particular. Leftovers always worked to bring the woman to life somewhat. 

 

“Hey, cold fries or reheated?” He asked. 

 

Agatha jumped, peaking over from under the hoodie to see him holding the container in the air. Without a word, she held her hand up. Billy brought it over, dropping on the couch beside her with a sigh.

 

“How you feeling?” 

 

Agatha grunted, shrugging the blanket off her shoulders to open the container up. She tossed a fry in her mouth, holding the next one up for him to take. 

 

They shared the fries in silence, watching the TV that played a crime documentary. Billy waited for a moment before asking, 

 

“Love triangle case?”

 

“Wife and new guy killed ex husband”

 

“Classic..” He muttered. “Why can’t people just get divorced?” 

 

“Why are people ever in love anyway?” 

 

The question wasn’t abnormal. Agatha always made fun of the idiots ruining their lives over someone. However, Billy noted the tone in her voice was different. Kate made a comment as well how Agatha screamed lesbian drama all over her. Billy didn’t say anything to them about her. Only a simple, 

 

“She gets wicked migraines. Bad timing” 

 

All while knowing physically, Agatha was fine. Kate was right. This weighed heavier than that. Also Billy didn’t magically forget what Agatha said in the car, how she acted when the subject of Rio came up. 

 

“That uh,” He scratched the back of his neck, adjusting in his spot with a shrug. “Sounds personal..”

 

Agatha was picking up a french fry as he spoke. She froze mid air, not turning her head or offering a verbal response. After a few seconds she continued on eating. Obviously ignoring the words he just spoke. 

 

He rolled his eyes, arms crossed tight against his chest. Billy almost caved, gave up and didn’t push Agatha to talk. This time though? 

 

No. 

 

“Agatha” He started, voice trembling a bit with fear. “I think I deserve something-”

 

“Deserve?” She snorted. “You fucking deserve?”

“Yes!” He exclaimed. “I brought you back food, I’m covering for you so you can stay here when you’re obviously not sick and-”

 

“Billy..” 

 

“And I’m also worried about you!” He finished, taking deep breaths while shaking his head. “You treat me like this little kid who can’t handle anything..most of the time, anyway, but!”

 

Billy sat forward, looking over to see Agatha slouching into the hoodie more. She mindlessly nibbled on the end of her fry, trying to focus on the TV and avoid his glare burning through her. 

 

“I’ve never seen you like this”

 

“I’m coming down with a cold” She lied. 

 

“No, I’ve seen you sick before” He pointed out. “We had Covid together once. Remember? You got it from me? And that stomach virus too and-”

“You’re not though, Agatha” He argued.

“Is it a family trait for you to be so annoying?”

“Is this Rio related?” He asked. 

 

Shit. 

Fuck. 

Shit.

Oh, and also? Fuck!

Well, he often hid the eyeroll. But as he aged, learned Agatha did in fact have a soft spot for him- He felt more confident to let his own attitude slip. 

 

“Exactly”

 

“Exactly nothing, idiot” She muttered, crossing her arms like a child pouting for not getting what they wanted. 

 

“Oh, right,” He nodded, clicking his tongue with another roll of his eyes. “That’s why you’re pouting right now”

But after stupid Kate?

After realizing she’d never be able to live a life without loving Rio, ignoring her own feelings, ever again?

 

“I’m not in the mood for your shit” She hissed.

“Life isn’t fair, twat”

 

“Dick would make more sense for me, but whatever. That’s not the point here” 

 

God, she made him a version of herself. The more time passed on, he developed a witty attitude of his own. Most of the time, Agatha was proud of him. Though when it was aimed her way?

“That you’re residing in Hell and I’m just visiting to either A, check in or B, get you out of it”

You know him better than that. 

 

“Agatha-”

 

“William, I swear to God”

 

“Oooh, full name? Now I’m in trouble, huh?”

 

Agatha huffed. “I miss when you’d nearly pee your pants when I’d say your name like that”

Of course, her words turned to bite her in the ass. Why should she even be surprised?

 

“So again, I will ask-”

 

“Think about if you value your life before doing so”

 

“Is-”

 

“William”

 

“This-”

 

“Do not make me kill you”

 

“Related to-”

“Rio?”

“I’m going to kill you”

Rio.

Rio. 

 

“And put up with you being an asshole-”

 

“Ri-”

 

Agatha almost said it. She cleared her throat, coughing excessively to try and disguise the word. Billy (Unfortunately for her) caught it with glee. 

 

“Knew it!” He jumped in his spot, clapping his hands. “I knew it! This is lesbian coded all across the board and-”

 

“You know absolutely nothing, idiot. You're clueless beyond repair. Delusional, actually”

 

“You said Ri-”

 

“You need a hearing test” 

 

“And you need to lie better” 

 

Agatha scoffed. “I lie perfectly, actually” 

 

“Not since the Rio situation..” 

 

Great. Another thing that bitch ruined about me. Agatha thought to herself. 

 

She had always been a great liar. A con artist who manipulated anyone she pleased. Yet Rio… shit. Once again, Agatha lost another piece to what made Agatha, her.

 

Now she was even more a ghost of the old Agatha Harkness. The woman she dreamt of being was left in the rearview mirror. The more time went on, the farther the car drove and her old self grew smaller in the 

 

“No. There's no situation ” 

 

Agatha tried to lie (And failed, again). 

 

“She- We hate each other. Always have, always will and-”

 

“Oh, so enemies to lovers?” He smiled. “I love those stories. Actually, it was my top trope for all I read last year and-”

 

“Kid,” She sighed. “It isn’t that”

 

“I know it when I see it” He said. “Even if you won’t tell me..” 

 

Agatha swallowed the lump in her throat. Enemies to lovers. It sounded beautiful to her. Everything she ever dreamed had come to profusion and…

 

I lost it. 

 

Not yet, no. She was still willing to put up a fight…just, well… delayed. 

 

“Agatha, I don’t know what it is with you two” 

 

He started, clearly debating his next words. No longer arguing or quickly shooting his own sarcastic replies. 

 

“But I think you two should sort this out. You’re..I’ve always thought you two would make sense together. Honestly” 

 

She pulled her lips back, picking at the skin off her thumb harder. Agatha always had a bad habit of doing so. She'd pick them till they bled, left scars and hangnails. 

 

“And if you ever want to talk? My lips are sealed. I wouldn’t utter a word on it” 

 

She knew he wouldn't. The kid could ramble on about some things in life, but when it came down to it? Something personal, serious such as Rio? 

 

Billy muttered about how he wanted to go to bed. He stood, stretching his back while almost on the verge of whispering his good night. 

 

Agatha without a doubt was frustrated and annoyed with him. The entire Rio situation in itself didn't help. However, she had to let him know one thing.

 

“Hey, kid” Agatha said. 

 

Billy turned. Hopeful eyes, wish filled voice that prayed Agatha would open up to him.

 

“Yeah?” He tried to hide his excitement, nervous to scare Agatha off. “What uh- What's up?” 

 

Agatha paused for a moment. She twitched her lips to the side, rolling her shoulders back while taking in a deep breath. Billy felt the seconds lasted hours while Agatha felt it was too soon, not able to fully think through her words. 

 

“You know..” She looked up, offering a soft smile that made Billy feel at ease. “Proud of you. You’re really starting to grow a pair of balls there. Not taking shit and backing down so easy anymore” 

 

He paused, momentarily upset it wasn't Agatha opening up about Rio. Though, he smiled softly himself. Sure it wasn't exactly what he was looking for. And the compliment may sound brutal for the way Agatha worded it. 

 

But if Billy learned anything about Agatha? The words held a stronger, heavier, deeper meaning than anyone would ever know. 

 

His cheeks turned red with a little smile. The boy nodded, gesturing a salute that made Agatha roll her eyes. 

 

“I’m learning from the toughest woman alive. Only makes sense” 

 

She snorted, shaking her head. 

 

“Night, Agatha” He said. 

 

Agatha smiled. “Night, kid” 

 

He exited the room, walking down the hall till his bedroom door echoed in the distance. 

 

Agatha was left alone once again. Rio felt heavier on her mind this time around. Then again Agatha had to laugh because- 

 

Is that even possible? 

 

 

The weekend had gone by painfully slow for Rio. No alcohol made her sleep through it, no matter how many episodes of Glee or South Park she forced herself to watch. It all went by at an agonizing pace. 

 

By Monday, Rio thought things would get somewhat better. She hated the idea of facing Agatha at work, but at least she got to lay eyes on her and maybe corner her into talking. 

 

Then Monday went by with no Agatha. 

 

Tuesday happened, no Agatha. 

 

By Wednesday when there was again- No Agatha. Rio had enough. It was close to noon when she debated abandoning her classes, storming to Agatha's apartment, breaking down the door- Whatever it took. 

 

She was stuck in her head stomping down the hall, ignoring anything Lilia had to say. Something about meetings and a possible work trip to Florida down the line. 

 

“Miami, yeah. Sounds great” 

 

Rio had muttered, not realizing what was being said. Instead she was just brushing her off to try and focus on getting through the day. 

 

Though as they passed the computer lab, Rio heard the copier being smacked a few times. 

 

Billy. 

 

Oh, that kid was a blessing for her at that moment. She hadn't tracked him down either. Some days he was too busy running around and Rio had been locked in her classroom to provide extra help with some students. 

 

She waved Lilia off, saying how they'd talk later. Luckily the older woman didn't put up a fight. 

 

Rio shoved her phone in her back pocket, sliding beside Billy who lit up instantly. 

 

“Oh, thank God. I hate this copier so much and-”

 

Like usual, Rio smacked it to fix it for him. Billy always called it the ‘Vidal Touch!’ But this time? It didn't just end with a small interaction. 

 

And the smack wasn't light either. 

 

The copier kicked into action after it was hit twice. Billy sighed in relief. He was about to thank her when his second worst nightmare became reality. 

 

“Thank you as always, Professor. I really appreciat-” 

 

“Tell me where Harkness is” 

 

Rio was leaning against the copier, holding the top down so he couldn't have access to the paper he needed. She didn't care if she came across mean, scary, any of it. He dealt with Agatha on the daily. The kid should be used to it by now. 

 

His lips parted, eyes wide as his body started to tremble. Sure, he had confidence with Agatha. But that was different! He had grown close to her. 

 

Not to mention, Rio was the strictest professor in the entire building. She had her nice moments, yes. Yet, Billy still barely knew her. 

 

Unfortunately, what did he know? Something was going on with the professors and he kept getting tossed in the middle. 

 

“What does that mean?” Rio pointed.

 

“What does what mean?” He rushed. 

 

“Your face is burning redder than a god damn apple. Where is she?”

 

Billy silently cursed his body out for its betrayal. That'd always been one of his weak spots. Agatha called him out all the time for it. Embarrassment, fear, even being giddy- His skin turned a fire red. Always dead set on giving his emotions away. 

 

He took in a deep breath, trying to let Agatha's words about being more confident echo in his mind. 

 

“Listen-”

 

“I'm listening if you tell me where the hell she is” 

 

“How would I know?!” 

 

“Because she was with you the rest of this weekend. You're back, she isn't. So where-”

 

“You both won't tell me what's going on with you. So, why keep tossing me in the middle?!” 

 

He had a point. Rio somewhat felt bad for him since he had been getting tossed in the middle. Then again, her sympathy was wiped away. 

 

‘You both won't tell me’

 

“What does both won't tell you mean?” 

 

Billy stared for a second before shaking his head. 

 

“I- Just..what it means, Professor. She won't tell me, you won't tell me-”

 

“Tell you what? What isn't she saying?” 

 

“I don't know!” He exclaimed. “All I know is clearly something happened between you two” 

 

“But how did you get to that conclusion if she hasn't said a word?” 

 

Billy scoffed, earning a glare from Rio. Luckily, he dodged it and forced himself to continue on. 

 

“I know when I see lesbians, okay?” He asked. “Besides, you pestering me for her address then she's in a mood twenty four seven after- I mean!” 

 

He gestured his hands in the air with a nervous laugh. 

 

“Professor Vidal, I don't mean to sound intrusive- I really don't. But the writing is on the wall here” 

 

Her tongue pushed the inside of her cheek, looking away to think over his words. 

 

Fine. Maybe they didn't hide this one so well. Then again, what did he mean by Agatha being in a mood . 

 

Is she mad at me? 

Is she as upset as I am? 

What is-

 

“All I know is Agatha wasn't feeling well” He said. “Otherwise, I'm just clueless in the middle here” 

 

She looked back over, fingertips drumming on top of the copier. He nervously looked over, lips twitched to the side as he started to rock back and forth on his feet. 

 

“Professor uh, I hate to…ask this, but” 

 

Rio could laugh at the way he slipped back into his usual self. A bundle of nerves, constantly hesitant to reply or ask for anything. 

 

She took pity on him by answering his question without needing to be asked. Her hand pushed off the copier, allowing him to grab the original sheet instantly. 

 

“Thank you,” He sighed in relief. “Professor Kale is-”

 

“A pain in the ass about timing, yes” Rio nodded. 

 

Billy weakly smiled with a small laugh. He glanced up to see Rio with her arms crossed, foot tapping on the floor as she glared at the ceiling. 

 

It was clear to him Rio was in the same spot as Agatha. She just seemed to turn to anger instead of wallowing in the darkness of her apartment. Agatha was doing just that last he knew. 

 

“She should be back tomorrow,” Billy said. “I promise. That's all I know” 

 

Rio nodded, offering a weak smile that barely existed. If he wasn't so close, he wouldn't have spotted it. 

 

He returned the same smile before turning around, heading to the door. However, he paused- Hand above the handle, mind pulling it's own tug of war game until he couldn't hold back any longer. 

 

“Professor Vidal?” 

 

The young man turned, seeing Rio shoot her eyes up to meet his. Billy didn't waste a second. He had her attention, the confidence radiating through him to speak. Now was his chance to add in his own thoughts before the window closed. 

 

“Although I may not know what has happened between you two..” 

 

Rio went to stop him, but he beat her to it before she could. 

 

“Agatha cares..” 

 

He spoke with true honesty. Even if he were a stranger, Rio would know he wasn't telling a lie. 

 

“That much is very clear and..I know I haven't known her forever, but..” 

 

Billy shrugged, now pushing down on the handle to prepare for Rio to kick him out. Agatha would have by now. And if Rio was just the same? Well-

 

“Thank you” Rio whispered. 

 

Shock was an understatement to describe what he felt in that moment. He was frantically searching for a reply, but it felt like his brain had hit a wall. Nothing in him was prepared to be met with that. 

 

He had told himself silently Rio would fight, tell him to fuck off. The scariest, strictest professor in the entire university truly wouldn't put up with him. 

 

Her response as well only made Billy realize how deep this was going between them. It was heavier than just lesbian drama. Something happened and he was desperate to know what it was. 

 

Obviously, yes. It was related to them being lesbians, but it was nothing light hearted. This wasn't about some friends with benefits situation. Not two co-workers that shared a drunken kiss or whatever. 

 

Billy wasn't necessarily a mind reader, but he could see it in both of the women's eyes. And he almost voiced it. He almost said the words aloud, 

 

“You're in love” 

 

Luckily Rio spoke before he could do so. 

 

She cleared her throat, waving him off with a strong, 

 

“Move it along now. You don't want Kale being more annoying than she already is” 

 

He snapped out of his little trance. Quick nods, hushed whispers of agreement while rushing down the hall. 

 

Just like Agatha a few nights before, he had left Rio behind to her lonesome. She moved to lean against the copier, hands running through her hair and tugging gently at the roots. 

 

Fuck.

 

The biggest word running through her mind was simply just… fuck.

 

What else was there to say? Billy was one of the only closest people to Agatha. If she never wanted to talk to her again, he would know. He would have told her as well to back off. Agatha was known to put him up to that. 

 

Instead not only did he break the news she'd be back to work the following day. Which really should be Rio's main focus. He also mentioned how- 

 

Agatha cares. 

 

Rio could cry over those two words alone. Although if she cared, why the hell wasn't she here? Why was Agatha still ignoring her and acting like they hadn't just confessed love, spent weeks on end together? 

 

Sure, she ran off. That's what started this whole mess. Then again if she cared..

 

Why are we playing this game? 

 

Rio shook her head, muttering a few, 

 

“Nope, nope” to herself on repeat. 

 

She pulled her phone out, thumbs trembling as she typed the words. Something Rio never did. Not even when she was sick, out of town, in a hospital room or even away for a funeral. 

 

For Agatha Harkness, Rio had done the unimaginable- 

 

“Classes for the rest of the day are canceled. Going home sick. Will keep everyone posted” 

 

The world's most strictest professor. 

 

The professor who never missed a day if she didn't have to and always expected her students to do the same. 

 

Arguably the most dedicated professor in the university had canceled her classes..

 

All for Agatha Harkness. 

 

Rio rushed to grab her belongings before anyone could find out she was not sick. As she raced through the hall, nearly broke down her classroom door- Rio started to realize slowly, 

 

She ruined me.

 

The woman had worked nonstop all her life. She took her career seriously to the point it fell to the level of life or death. And now? 

 

Her classes were canceled solely to show up on Agatha's doorstep all over again. 

 

God, what have I become? 

 

She locked the classroom door behind her, chasing outside to her car. Rio didn't care if her laptop broke from how aggressively her bag was tossed in the passenger seat. The woman almost forgot her seatbelt as she put the car in drive. 

 

“This is ridiculous..” She laughed to herself. 

 

What the hell am I doing?

 

Rio didn't care if Agatha didn't want to see her. She had no choice at this rate. Days without a reply, suddenly not showing up for work and Billy revealing- 

 

Agatha cares. 

 

She'd gone mad, truly. Part of her debated tossing away her entire career if it meant she could camp out on Agatha's doorstep till this was fixed. The woman realized even more how she changed as that thought ran across her mind. 

 

Rio only cared about work, yes. Everyone knew that. But Rio also never chased anyone. If they wanted to be in her life, so be it. If they didn't, she'd let them go. 

 

Yes, letting people go had hurt her. But it was never this. She never felt the rage or need to chase them down. When it came to Agatha though? Rio was already planning how she'd keep the cops at bay holding her hostage in the apartment. 

 

Agatha was hers and maybe that sounded possessive and psycho, but Rio didn't care. She'd take time later on to face who she had become. 

 

For now? She was fed up. And Agatha didn't have a choice but to face her now. 

 

You're mine, Harkness.

 

“Agatha! Open up!” 

 

Rio had barely stepped foot in front of Agatha's door when she started to pound her arm against it. After the first few times when there was no reply, she matched her voice to tell the demand. 

 

And still, there was nothing. 

 

She groaned, almost ready to kick the door in herself. 

 

“Agatha, come on. I'm fucking tired of playing this game!” 

 

Rio waited, clenching her fist and looking down the hall to see an older woman glaring at her. She rolled her eyes and paid no mind. 

 

Agatha Harkness was her future wife. Rio would make a fool of herself to assure that would be a reality. 

 

She pounded on the door again. This time instead of being able to say anything, the woman down the hall yelled out, 

 

“She isn't home!” 

 

Rio jumped, suddenly thinking how the older woman wasn't so bad. Maybe she had some information for her to work with. 

 

“Do you know where she went?” 

 

“Errands-”

 

“Okay, errands. Cool. But where?” 

 

She shrugged. “I don't know that much, dear. All I know is we said our hellos and she's been gone for the day” 

 

Rio took in a deep breath, wiping her hand across her forehead while the other lifted up as a small unspoken, thanks . The older woman smiled, disappearing into her apartment right after. 

 

Great. Alright, well, fine. So she isn't home? Doable. I can camp out here. Totally. 

 

Rio thought she had been saying all of that in her mind, but the words were mumbled out. Luckily no one was around to hear. 

 

She fiddled with her fingers, pacing for more than ten minutes. Back and forth, over and over and to no surprise-

 

Still no Agatha. 

 

“Where the hell are you, Harkness?” Rio muttered. 

 

She pulled out her phone to text again, but when Agatha's face on the contact ID came up? That's when the memory hit her. 

 

Agatha told her one time if she ever wanted to swing by her place (Even though they always stayed at her's) how there was-

 

“A spare key above the door frame” She muttered to herself. 

 

Rio pushed up on the tips of her toes, reaching blindly and swiping her hand side to side. The dust built on her fingers. Rio swore she hit a dead bug. Maybe a spiderweb as well, but fuck she didn't know and didn't care to know. 

 

Like a beacon, the best feeling in the world-

 

“Yes!” 

 

Rio bounced as the metal touched her fingers. She pulled it off, looking down at the bronze key shining up at her. The woman wiped the dust off, quickly making work to unlock the handle. 

 

Just as she turned the knob, took one step inside the apartment- Logic kicked in. 

 

Am I really doing this? 

Have I become this insane to break into someone's apartment? 

 

For all Rio knew, Agatha could be sleeping or home any second. She already looked obsessive texting her on repeat and leaving voicemails like some crazed ex who couldn't let go. 

 

The woman stepped back, staring at the door with fear coursing through her veins. 

 

What have I become? 

 

She'd been in love before, sure. But it never drove her to this point. Where she genuinely was considering breaking into a woman's apartment to do…

 

What exactly? 

 

“The fuck..” She muttered. 

 

What would breaking in even achieve? Especially if Agatha wasn't here and-

 

Make sure she didn't leave. 

 

Rio knew her brain was grasping at delusional straws, but it worked. Plus! It wasn't breaking in if she had a key. She wasn't picking the lock or whatever…right? 

 

The mental gymnastics Rio was putting herself through would be hysterical to broadcast live for an audience. Agatha would actually love to be in those seats as well and-

 

Stop relating her to everything, dammit! Her mind yelled to herself. 

 

Yet, it felt impossible to follow through with that demand. 

 

She muttered a quick, “Fuck it” and did something- Crossed a line she never had been within a mile radius of before. 

 

Rio slid into Agatha's apartment, softly clicking the door shut behind her. 

 

This is it. I've hit a new low.

 

Well, if Agatha showed up and called the cops. At least Wanda was around to bail her out. 

 

She slid the key in her pocket, taking slow steps around the familiar apartment. Her eyes scanned every inch, seeing Agatha's belongings were still scattered. The furniture was still the same, dishes were left in the strainer (Agatha never left until all the dishes were clean. That was a rule Rio had to adjust to). 

 

All signs led to Agatha being back. She hadn't gone on another trip. If she did, she would have taken her purse that sat on the couch. The only way Rio knew she wasn't home was because her jacket and favorite pair of boots were missing. 

 

Rio knew it was time to leave. She got the answer she was looking for. Agatha was due to be back at the university by tomorrow. Rio could confront her there and this would all be either a memory they'd laugh over. 

 

Or, a memory Agatha would never know about. Most likely that one. 

 

Rio started to leave, but then her eyes caught the dining room table. She glanced over to the front door to make sure it wasn't opening. Really, Rio should look for places to hide in case that happened. 

 

Instead, the envelope on the table had caught her eye. 

 

She slowly approached it as if it was a bomb that'd explode. An item that'd catch her in the act. Rio leaned over, eyes skimming the neat hand writing that was far too familiar.

 

“Photos from our trip! Thanks for tagging along Agatha:)”

 

“Billy..” She mumbled to herself. 

 

There was a sigh of relief from that. It was just Billy and some photos from their trip. He'd always been a materialistic person. Before the summer, he always made sure to do his rounds and take photos with everyone. 

 

Rio obliged every time to make him happy, but always tossed the printed copy he sent aside. Not because she hated him or anything. She just wasn't sentimental for those kinds of things. 

 

Well, at least with anyone else. Agatha was different. Shocker. 

 

“Just Billy,” She shrugged. 

 

There was no more need to stay. Clearly Agatha was back, but truly out running errands. Rio was on a time clock to get the hell out before she was caught and ultimately lost Agatha forever. She wouldn't blame her for it either. 

 

She was about to turn when a force of wind pushed her back. A little peek at the photos wouldn't hurt. Just to confirm Agatha looked miserable without her. She wanted to see the, 

 

Agatha cares. 

 

For herself. 

 

The first few photos were of sunsets and nature trails. Agatha appeared in only a few photos. Mainly in the background and always at a restaurant or apartment. She didn't appear to join them on adventures. That wasn't shocking. 

 

One by one, Rio flipped through. It looked normal. Honestly, like they had a nice trip. 

 

That was until she flipped to a certain photo. One that made everything around her stop. Her heart sunk, stomach twisted and threatened to turn her inside out- Make her puke everything up on the table before her. 

 

A woman was sitting beside Agatha. Both focused on each other, laughing, heads close, oblivious to the rest of the table. 

 

Shit. 

 

“This is caring?” She muttered to herself, smacking the photo against the others with a stronger- “This is fucking caring?!” 

 

Her heart was pounding out of control. Rio felt her whole body run cold and hot at the same time. She'd been angry in her life before, but never to this extent. This was a new level of rage Rio didn't know was possible. 

 

And fuck, it scared her. 

 

Rio smacked down the rest of the photos. She folded the one, not caring how messy the crease in it would be. At that moment, she didn't care if Agatha found her. Rio knew the reason why she was being ignored now. 

 

While she was back home sobbing her eyes out, pleading for Agatha to answer and apologizing profusely for what happened. Agatha was moving on as if they never were in love to begin with. 

 

“Fucking bitch” Rio hissed. 

 

She started to storm out of the apartment, not caring to return the key to the top of the frame. Rio didn't bother to hide the evidence she had broken in. 

 

Luckily (More lucky for Agatha, really) the woman didn't show. Rio was able to leave the apartment building without being caught. 

 

She didn't know where to start. On one end, Rio wasn't surprised. The enemies to lovers trope was ridiculous and never realistic. Wanda was delusional for thinking the two would ever be more than just two women who hated each other. 

 

Agatha was a bitch. Agatha was annoying. Agatha Harkness made Rio Vidal's life a living hell and that would never fucking change. The photo in her hand proved it. 

 

Agatha cares. 

 

“Bull- fucking -shit, William!” 

 

Rio hissed aloud as if he was near. She continued on, earning a few weird stares from others in the parking lot as she charged to her car. 

 

“This is fucking caring?! This?” She laughed. “Fucking slut- I make one mistake ONE and this is how she-”

 

Rio clenched her fists, taking in a deep breath before letting out a yell as she kicked her driver's side door hard enough to make a dent in it. 

 

“Shit!” 

 

She wasn't sure what she'd regret more. How her knee would ultimately be aching for days from that or her car now having a dent in it. One she'd have to make up an excuse to not sound like some emo teenager with dramatic anger issues. 

 

Rio looked around, making sure Agatha hadn't seen her at all. Then like clockwork- The familiar car entered the lot. For a split second, Rio debated charging over and demanding answers. 

 

However, seeing Agatha briefly through the windshield? Rio's heart shattered. The anger dissolved into despair, regret for ever allowing herself to feel more than just attraction towards her. 

 

The woman rushed to hide in her car, even reclining the seat to do so. She held the photo back up without meaning to, glancing at it once more. 

 

Agatha's smile. She missed calling that look her very own, but..

 

It wasn't her smile anymore. Agatha wasn't Rio's. 

 

She fell in the arms of another woman. Rio made the worst decision of her life. If only she stayed, if she never ran or maybe she reached out way too many times. 

 

She dropped the photo, covering her face with her arms as sobs started to take control. Her body shook, bones nearly cracked under the pressure her emotions kept piling on. 

 

Agatha cares…

 

The thing is though, she didn't. Not in Rio's mind anymore..

Chapter End Notes

Poor Billy. Someone get him a shot of whiskey. Sheesh.

Smooth Criminals in Love

Chapter Notes

100k fucking words now. This was supposed to be like a two or three part fic..my bad LMAO

ANYWAY quick little back and forth chapter. You'll be twisting your head left to right until the end that sets up for a more slower pace. HOPE YOU LIKE IT UHHHH I can't think of anything else to say. Ty for reading:))) ENJOY!

"I hate myself for loving you
Can't break free from the the things that you do
I wanna walk but I run back to you
That's why I hate myself for loving you"

Agatha tossed her phone and keys on the kitchen counter. A dramatic sigh escaped her. One that was heavy, exhausted from the last few days. Between the trip, Rio, and battling with her own self as well as accepting who she was- 

 

She was beat. That was to say the least. 

 

The shopping bags were placed on the dining room table, peaking over to see the envelope Billy texted he had dropped off. She gave him a spare key a few months ago. The bar he liked to venture to was just down the block. Agatha scolded him for walking or taking an Uber home when her place was a safer option.  

 

She noticed the envelope opened. The photos sticking out somewhat. Though Agatha thought nothing of it. Billy probably wanted to look through them to make sure there were no duplicates. 

 

Always such a perfectionist..

 

She rolled her eyes, picking up the photos to look through them. Agata was relieved there wasn't a lot of her, but even more so nothing with Kate. 

 

If there was? She was going to toss it before it ever saw the light of day. Rio never needed to know about that. Even if nothing happened, the fact Billy blindly tried to set her up on a date stressed her out enough as it was. And she wanted to win Rio back. 

 

That would certainly not help if she ever were to find out. 

 

After looking through the photos, Agatha checked out the items she had bought. Retail therapy was always her form of self care. But this time? It was retail therapy- Rio edition. 

 

Agatha wouldn't say it was bribery, per say. In some people's eyes, sure. That was kind of exactly what she was doing. However, for her, this was normal. 

 

She already showered Rio with gifts. From bigger ones to simple little things. If she saw a little new snack Rio may like, she grabbed it. When Agatha saw a cool rock, she brought it home. New plants, new blankets. Etc, etc. 

 

Agatha's love language was gifts and that'd never change. 

 

She'd be a liar to say though this didn't hold a smidge of bribery at all. But still! Love language over bribery, always. 

 

There were three different pairs of boxers. Two had dinosaurs. The other had Dolly Parton. A stupid joke gift they'd both laugh over. Other things were snacks, small Lego kits, and a new hoodie that said the classic, 

 

“Best Dog Mom Ever” 

 

Her favorite shade of dark green as well. It was perfect. Agatha was content with what she had bought. There was an urge, little nudge for her to add one more thing. 

 

No. I can't. 

 

Agatha wasn't good with words. Yet, a letter seemed to be the best thing to add. She wanted it more than anything. To write how in love she was, put it into words, give something for Rio to hold onto. 

 

You don't know how to even say it half of the time.

Let alone have replied to her at all. 

 

Maybe a letter could happen down the line. That could be a goal for the future. But for now? Her second thought was right. Agatha's phone was staring up at her. The promise she made herself on the way home was waiting to be filled. 

 

Text her. Just. Text her. 

 

Agatha had repeated the words to herself all day. Really, more the last two, but kept pushing it off. Yet, she was due to be back on campus in less than twenty four hours. Maybe they could meet tonight and make things less awkward for tomorrow. 

 

She picked up her phone, typing a small message that told Rio how sorry she was for the late reply. Using the trip as an excuse, saying how exhausted she was. That was good, right? Had to be, Agatha told herself. It was small, cut straight to the point. She didn’t sound angry or anything in the slightest. 


Besides, trips were exhausting, no? Anyone would understand that. 

 

Who am I kidding? Agatha sighed.

 

It wouldn’t be that easy. Rio wouldn’t just come out of the woodworks with open arms, forgiving and all. As much as she wished for it, Agatha was well aware of how much of a selfish asshole she chose to be. Rio had every right to ignore her and offer the same treatment Agatha had given her.

 

She almost texted her again, but decided against it. Maybe giving Rio space was the best option. Allow her to make her own way back to Agatha. She’d still send another text in the morning, stop by her classroom, wait for her in the parking lot and-

 

Okay, fine. Maybe Agatha wouldn’t completely give Rio space, but was that a bad thing? Rio hadn’t given her space either. The last few hours had been the longest time her phone was silent. No new messages, voicemails, nothing. 

 

And right then, Agatha felt herself pushed off the edge. Not of glory either. This cliff was unnerving, terrifying. Agatha started to chew the hangnail on her thumb, foot tapping as she stared at the screen. 

 

She’s quiet. I fucked up. 

 

Part of her debated dropping everything and showing up on Rio’s doorstep that night. Who cared if Rio didn’t want her there? The regret was taking over like poison, threatening to end Agatha’s life before she knew it. 

 

No, no. Rio needed space. Agatha had to respect and give her that. If she wasn’t reaching out, that was her message and Agatha needed to get it through her head. 

 

She put her phone down, stepping away to head for the bathroom. A burning hot shower would bring her back down to earth. She’d be able to clear her head, make more logical decisions instead of acting on impulse and-

 

Rio changed me. 

 

Agatha was stripping her pants when the new found realization came to life. 

 

No longer was Agatha the spontaneous being she always was. Her mind was actually processing, thinking through not only the woman she was growing into- But no longer making choices with no thought behind them. 

 

Rio was always the logical one. Has that seriously rubbed off on her? Was she now slowly becoming a woman who thought before acting?

 

“Oh, what the fuck?” She muttered with a frustrated laugh. 

 

She knew allowing herself to love Rio would change things. Agatha chose to drop herself into the abyss, enter the unknown territory she avoided like a plague. What she didn’t realize was how it wouldn’t just be all about facing fears and life changes. 

 

Agatha Harkness was becoming someone she was not. Through and through, up, down, left, right and all of the above. 

 

Of course, parts of her old self clearly remained. The selfishness of ignoring Rio, trying to gift her way out of trouble, little things she hadn’t let go of quite yet. However, so much more of her was gone. 

 

And really… is that good?

 

Agatha’s hands covered her face, pushing back through her hair and took a deep breath. 

 

Did she regret falling in love with Rio? No. 

 

Did she regret not focusing on the little things sooner? How her personality had changed so she’d work on accepting those things sooner? Possibly, but then again- How was Agatha to know and expect that’d happen? 

 

Love was completely new to her. She had relationships in the past, but it never compared to this. Rio wasn’t just a new character in her life, she was a separate book. Not a small chapter, but a whole ‘nother saga. 

 

Agatha didn’t know the rules, but who did? She had to learn just like anyone else. Though after the last few days, Agatha could only wonder-

 

Am I too late?

Rio ignored Agatha’s text. She actually laughed over it when she read it. Not only from Agatha finally ending her radio silence with some pathetic excuse. But also?

 

The irony of it appearing the second she had pulled into her driveway after getting home from Agatha’s apart-

 

I broke into someone’s apartment. 

 

She felt the adrenaline shoot fire through her over the realization. Rio nearly slammed the car door hard enough to break the frame as she ran to hide in her house. Her heart was hammering, stomach turning as her skin vibrated with goosebumps all over. 

What have I done?

 

Since when did Rio fuckin’ Vidal not think through her ideas? She never made rash decisions. Was never one who acted on impulse. Had love actually driven her to the point of insanity? Could love do that to someone?

 

Rio hadn’t considered Agatha would have an effect on who she was. Sure, Agatha would change aspects of her life. But, change parts of her? Personality wise to who she was at her core. 

 

She never thought love would do this to her. Let alone Agatha Harkness would hold this kind of power. Sure, everyone knew Agatha was the definition of a manipulative witch. Rio saw right through the bullshit though. She wasn’t one who fell into the trap that easily.

 

And yet, she broke into a woman’s apartment solely from being ignored. 

 

The night dragged on from there. Rio had tossed and turned in bed, moved to the couch to snuggle with Nicky and try to sleep. However, there was no way her mind, anxiety, anything would allow it. 

 

Rio was terrified of who she was becoming. 

Rio feared how deep in love she was with someone. It was new, unknown to her. Sure, she had love before. But it wasn’t this. 

 

They weren’t Agatha. 

 

Around midnight is when Rio’s mind went from a smaller, easier level of alert to a maximum point she didn’t know existed. It was when she picked her phone up, seeing two missed calls and a voicemail. 

 

Rio tossed her phone down, refusing to listen. She wouldn’t give in that quick. Agatha didn’t deserve such satisfaction. And Rio would NOT let Agatha think of her as a pushover. Someone easy to manipulate, take advantage of, etc.

 

Five minutes passed when Rio was chewing on her thumb, side eyeing the phone until her hand quickly snatched it. 

 

She will never know I listened to it. 

 

Rio held Nicky close when she hit play. Just in case she needed to hide, he’d be her shield. The boy was her protector, safety, someone she relied on for comfort. He’d been the only one for years now to be that.

 

Until Agatha was here to be my second..

 

She hid her face in his fur while listening, mentally cursing the way his breathing and tail picked up at the sound of Agatha’s voice. 

 

“We’re mad at her, Nicky” Her voice was muffled into his body, but Agatha’s voice through the phone speaker was clear as day. 

 

“Rio..” 

 

She didn’t realize her small whimper that crept up her throat. Too busy hating how good her name sounded on Agatha’s tongue.

 

“I-..I get it. I do. You have every right to not speak to me” 

 

“Wow. She does know something for once..” Rio mumbled. 

 

“I should have replied, okay? I know that..just- This game we're playing is childish”

 

Rio’s eyes flew open, body sitting up as she screamed at the phone like Agatha could hear her.

 

“Childish? YOU STARTED IT!” 

 

“I just want things the way they were. Don’t you?” 

 

Rio laughed. She shot up to her feet, pacing with her hands gripping her hips like a tether to keep her grounded. 

 

“So..let’s just get this over with and-”

 

“Oh..you bitch ” She hissed. 

 

Rio grabbed her phone, ending the voicemail before it was over. She was ready to call or text- Curse Agatha out, call her on the manipulative tone and dismissive words. There was never even an apology! Agatha was prancing around the word like it was invisible, sworn off into oblivion. 

 

“How hard is it to say fucking sorry?” She muttered. 

 

No. Agatha does not deserve her attention at all. Maybe if she apologized, Rio would be willing to reach out. Alas, she wasn't going to let the anger drive her into insanity. 

 

Not that it already hadn't, of course. 

 

She tossed her phone back on the couch, apologizing under her breath to Nicky for almost hitting his back with it. He just snored a bit, clueless to how his Mom was on the verge of committing murder. 

 

Oh, how nice. Break in AND murders now? Lovely..

 

Rio started to bite on her thumb. The hangnail that was close to breaking off, dripping a tad of blood and would sting for the next couple of days. As annoying as that'd be? It'd still hurt less than what Rio was going through at that moment. 

 

Agatha had ignored her. 

She had broken into a woman's apartment, stole a photo which made her feel psychotic-

 

But she cheated. Did she though? 

 

They hadn't made anything super official. Nothing was ever vocalized or in writing. But, she had just confessed she was in love with her! They were both in love, Rio thought. 

 

She was left wondering more if this was some prank. Would Agatha laugh in her face when they saw each other in the hall? Did she lie through her teeth or was just bored and stringing her along? 

 

Rio shook her head. She didn't want to know. The break in, obsessive thoughts, texts and calls. It was all too much. They had rushed into it. Crashed and burned before they were able to keep the fire alive for more than what felt like two seconds. 

 

She was never one to rush into things either. Rio Vidal was logical, took time to process and build up relationships even with friends. It was a reason her life was limited to a small social circle. She had to build trust, connection and all of the above. 

 

Yet with Agatha…everything was like a surge of power, faster than the speed of light. The only slow build up to exist was the bickering and hating each other for a few short years. 

 

Next thing Rio knew, Agatha was in her life. She borderline resided in her house. The woman built a home for herself in Rio's heart and took over her mind like a parasite. 

 

It was all so beautiful until it wasn't. Rio's walls were back up. Higher than before, stronger than ever. She wouldn't allow herself to gracefully fall back into Agatha's arms. Part of her wanted to completely shun Agatha, swear her off like a drug she would never touch again. 

 

And yet, as Rio picked up her phone to block Agatha's number. With the contact ID profile picture smiling up at her. Agatha with Nicky, smiling into his fur with Rio's cardigan wrapped around her. Her hands trembled, eyes stung with tears on the horizon. 

 

She couldn't make the promise to herself that Agatha was gone for good. However, Rio could do one thing. 

 

I'm not going back that easy. 

“Keep it up, kid” 

 

It's Agatha. 

Shit. 

 

Rio froze when the voice echoed in the hall behind her. The raspy tone that never failed to send shivers down her spin. Even in the midst of her anger, resentment- Agatha still held the power to take a breath and have an effect on her. 

 

She had blocked Agatha's number the night before. So close to cancelling classes, but decided against it. One, Lilia would actually kill her. Two? Agatha wasn't going to hold power over her. Well, at least not all of the power. 

 

Rio was going to work as she did before. She existed in a workplace where once she had tolerated, ignored, and dealt with Agatha's existence before loving her. It'd be simple to do it all over again. Loving Agatha didn't have to mean being co-workers would be different, right? 

 

Sworn enemies, the two co workers everyone knew to not expect to stay in the same room. They could be that again with no issue. 

 

I can learn to hate her again. 

 

“The more you practice, the easier it becomes. You'll be speaking to crowds that spread for miles by the time you know it” Agatha said. 

 

The young man chuckled, voice clearly showing his nerves were radiating through him. That was typical. Even the students that felt most comfortable in Professor Harkness's classroom were still intimidated by her somewhat. 

 

“Well, I don't think I'll ever be a politician drawing out those kind of numbers”

 

“Not with that attitude, you won't” Agatha said. 

 

“But-”

 

“No buts,” She cut him off, voice clipped and left no room for a debate. “Don't you dare question your talent. You've got a good head on those shoulders. Use it ” 

 

She heard his laugh, listening to how they both shared a soft goodbye. And fuck.. Rio hated what that did to her. 

 

Not only hearing Agatha’s voice, knowing she was just down the hall from her- But it was no longer just a small, meaningless sight to see how encouraging Agatha was. When before Rio would find it nice, but nothing more than that. Now? 

 

She's incredible. 

 

It made her heart swell with a warm sense of pride to know Agatha Harkness. The woman who was tough on the outside, full of insults and sarcastic remarks. When it all really boiled down to it? Agatha had a heart of pure (stupid) fucking gold. 

 

She wanted the best for her students. She tried her hardest to make people laugh on their worst days (Even if Agatha didn't think anyone noticed). And even worse for Rio to realize?

 

She took care of me. 

 

She loved…me. 

 

Did she though? 

 

Rio let her forehead rest against the door for a moment, resisting the urge to slam it against the hardwood until she passed out. 

 

God, Rio didn’t have time for this shit. Nor the energy or strength in her to make it through. But…she had to. Rio had students who relied on her, a career she had given up her entire soul for. 

 

It’d be fine..it had to be. 

She shook her head, trying to rid Agatha from her completely. Of course, that'd never work. If it did, Rio would have done that years ago (She’d preach that till the world’s end). 

 

“Fuck” She muttered, thinking much worse in her head. 

 

But if Rio let those words free? The entire campus would hear her loud and clear.  

 

The woman was about to make a left turn down the hall. She'd take the longer way to the parking lot to avoid risking an interaction with Agatha. However, it didn't go her way. 

 

Rio sighed seeing the caution tape and cones up. Her eyes looked around for the custodian, repair guy, whoever to tell her if it was safe to cross or not. Then again, maybe she didn't care if it was safe. Anything felt more secure than walking past Agatha Harkness's room. 

 

She held tighter on her bag, moving to step over the caution tape when there was a laugh behind her. Rio jumped, nearly fell backwards at the sound. 

 

“Dumbass” Alice said. 

 

The woman grinned wide, Rio rolled her eyes. 

 

“I wouldn't go that way-”

 

“Why?” Rio huffed. 

 

“Kid vomited all over the place. They just cleaned it up, but are coming back to make sure it's-”

 

Rio gagged, hands in the air. “Please stop talking” 

 

Alice laughed. “Yeah, figured you wouldn't want to step in that. Even if it looks clean” 

 

She ran a hand through her hair, ripping her eyes away. Rio always felt sick at the thought of vomit. Maybe more extreme than others, but still. The only one she could imagine being able to tough her reaction through would be for Nicky and Ag-

 

One. Nicky is one. Agatha doesn't- No. She is not included. Stop that. 

 

Rio needed another plan. Something quick to avoid having to see Agatha. 

 

I could just hide until she leaves? 

 

No, some nights Agatha stayed late especially if she was out for a day or two. That wouldn't work. 

 

Kill myself?

 

Nicky needs his mom, unfortunately. Wanda would also bring her back to life just to kill her again. Waste of time. 

 

She peaked up to see Alice texting someone back. Rio felt the lightbulb go off then. 

 

“Alice!” Rio said, pointing at her. 

 

“What's up?” Alice asked. 

 

“I'm heading out for the night. Wanna’ go grab a drink?” 

 

Rio didn't want to be social, but asking meant Alice would walk down the hall and out to the parking lot wirh her. It'd be perfect. Rio could be distracted speaking to someone else and Agatha wouldn't pressure her to stay back and-

 

“I can't” Alice shrugged.

 

Shit.

 

“I'm heading over to Jen's room right now for uh, extra help with something”

 

Rio pushed her tongue in her cheek, arms folded with an amused, 

 

“Uh-huh” 

 

Alice blushed, hand rubbing the back of her neck as she took steps away. Even if Rio was panicking on the inside? This was beautiful and entertaining as all hell. 

 

The two had been sneaking around, that much was clear. Both hiding it, but failing more and more each day. 

 

“Can you two just admit you're-”

 

“Later, Vidal!” Alice waved, nearly running down the hall at a high rate of speed. 

 

Rio snickered, but the humorous distraction was short lived. She still needed a plan, an escape. Luckily for her, footsteps started to pace down the hall with papers rustling along. 

 

“Hey kid” Rio stepped forward, cutting into his path. 

 

Billy looked up from the mess in his arms. A flicker of worry crossed his face. She couldn't blame him for that. 

 

“Yes, professor?” He asked. 

 

“Where you heading?” 

 

“Uh, Professor Harkness's room..” 

 

His voice became smaller as he said the name. Once again, Rio couldn't blame him for being hesitant. She would be as well if she were in his shoes. 

 

Rio nodded, gesturing down the hall. “Great. I'll walk with you” 

 

Billy stood a bit taller, head tilted as his lips parted to say something. She didn't give him the chance to do so. 

 

Instead Rio turned, hearing him catch up to walk by her side. As they took the turn down the hall, Agatha still stood against her doorframe with another student. 

 

Her arms were folded, glasses perched on the bridge of her nose. The secondary back up pair that only reminded Rio how she still had Agatha's main pair on her nightstand. She was busy revising a paper in her hand, nodding along to whatever the student was saying. 

 

“And then Lilia wanted me to make sure everyone signed up for-”

 

“Yeah, sure” Rio nodded, taking the clipboard from him. 

 

Billy had been rambling on about something. Truthfully, Rio wasn't listening. Something about Lilia's retirement at the end of the year. A get together of sorts, Rio didn't know or care. 

 

Her attention was on Agatha who was now smiling. She gave the paper back with a nod, hands waving in the air as she rambled on. 

 

Every step took them closer and closer. Rio's nerves began to turn her limbs into nothing but tremors. Her fingers struggled to quickly sign her name before passing the clipboard back to Billy. 

 

It was a countdown till death. A never ending walk that felt as if it stretched for miles. As they were just two doors down, the student and Agatha said their goodbyes and-

 

“Agatha!” Billy called out. 

 

Fuck. 

 

Agatha looked right at her first. The soft teaching gaze filled with wisdom and encouragement shifted into something smaller. 

 

Rio watched her tense, stand taller. How she started to fidget with her fingers, cross her arms only to uncross them a second after. 

 

In another world, a different time, Rio would find the sight adorable. How she didn't know what to do, how to hold herself. 

 

But, that wasn't the case. Not anymore. 

 

“I just wanted to stop by and-”

 

Agatha leaned over, taking a step forward as she ignored the young man completely. 

 

“Rio, hey” Agatha breathed. 

 

Her voice had unsurprisingly 

changed. No longer the teaching one. It was the familiar softness Rio had become accustomed to overtime. Only now, she could hear the pain and regret through each word. 

 

Don't give in. 

 

“I've been calling. Are you-”

 

“I gotta’ go” Rio held her hand up. 

 

The woman couldn't look at Agatha as she spoke. Her feet stormed down the hall, chest tight as her pulse was racing faster than ever. 

 

It was tempting to turn, push Agatha in her classroom and slam the door behind. Maybe to bitch her out, maybe to kiss her, maybe to fuck her senseless right then and there to claim her again. 

 

Instead, behind her she left Agatha to watch her leave. The doors clicked open and slammed shut. Echoed down the hall, made Agatha jump and rip her eyes away from the vacant space Rio had stood in. 

 

As if Agatha watching Rio, Rio seeing Agatha, all of it wasn't awkward enough? The professor's attention turned to her left, seeing the young man frightened out of his own mind. 

 

Any other time, Agatha would laugh. The boy seemingly saw a ghost, frozen in his stance of fear. Though after just watching who felt like the love of her life storm off? 

 

Agatha sighed. “What's up?” 

 

She turned as she spoke, walking back to her desk as Billy's feet stumbled in behind. 

 

“Uh, are you two-”

 

“William, do you value your life?” 

 

She rounded her desk, fingers skimming along the edge while her eyes glanced up over the rim of her glasses. 

 

He swallowed his nerves down, nodding while rushing the words out. 

 

“I'm stopping by with the final sign up sheet. Just a confirmation for the tr-”

 

“Give it” 

 

She held her hand up, grabbing the pen off her desk to quickly sign right under the name, 

 

Rio Vidal. 

 

“Jesus..” She muttered, forcing the clipboard back. Nearly hitting his chest while doing so. “Is that it?” 

 

Her voice was rough, clipped. A sharp edge that represented a sword filled with vengeance. Billy wasn't even the target, but still felt the brutal attack that was meant for Professor Vidal instead. 

 

“Uh, yes. Yeah” He stammered, packing his bag while turning on his heel. “Have a good night, Agatha” 

 

She hummed, focusing on packing her own belongings when she snapped her fingers. 

 

"Shit” 

 

He turned around with a quick, “Yes?” 

 

She sighed, looking up at him with a tired glare. Yet it was gentle, struggling to remain calm for the innocent soul before her. 

 

“I need my spare key back” 

 

Billy didn't hesitate to agree. He nodded, smiling softlg. 

 

“Yeah, I can keep an eye out for it. No prob-"

 

That's when her temper ran short. It wasn't directly Billy's fault. The kid was always forgetful, scatter brained just as she was. But between Rio, never sleeping, and constantly stressed the last few days. 

 

Agatha sighed, eyes closed as she shook her head. 

 

"William, did you seriously lose a key again?"

 

"What?” He asked, shaking his head. “No, no. I-”

 

Fucks sake. 

 

“Honey, you dropped the photos off by my place and now the spare key I keep on my door frame is gone. I understand if you needed it, but if you lost it again, I-”

 

She heard the soft jingle that made her look back up. In the air, Billy held his keychain. The exact blue coated one Agatha had given him shined in the fluorescent light.

 

“You gave me mine," He said. “Remember?”

 

Agatha stared, drumming her fingertips along the edge of her desk. Her lips pulled back, mind clouded and frustrated. 

 

After a few moments she nodded, unable to argue with him any further on it. The evidence was before her, his key right there with no need to use the spare one. 

 

She continued to pack her belongings while Billy spoke. He was saying something along the lines of how maybe it fell or she misplaced it, but Agatha knew the key was never touched. Not even Rio used it when Agatha informed her on where it was. 

 

“I’ll still keep an eye out for it though. Goodnight, Agatha!” He smiled. 

 

“Yeah,” Agatha muttered, hand running through her hair as she added a low, “Night..”

 

Her classroom door shut, leaving her to drop in the chair behind her. She pressed her palm over her mouth, staring into the distance as her mind raced through the question,

 

Where the hell did that key go?

Agatha stepped through the elevator onto her apartment floor. The bag weighed heavy on her shoulders. 

 

Books, papers, her laptop and iPad all ready to be lived on for her to catch up on work she was behind. 

 

A wine bottle was tucked under her arm, promising to ease her mind for the rest of the night. 

 

Agatha was happy to be home. No more using her voice, faking being happy and draining energy that already didn't exist. She started to unlock her door when one opened down the hall. Not a second later did Agatha hear a soft, 

 

“Hey, sweetie” Sharon smiled.

 

As much as she didn't want to talk, Agatha didn't have it in her to be a bitch. Call it the Rio Vidal broken heart effect or whatever, she assumed. 

 

Agatha looked over her shoulder with a weak smile. 

 

“Evening” 

 

“Did that young woman ever get to you?” Sharon asked. 

 

What? 

 

“Who?” Agatha asked, taking a step back to face her. 

 

“The one from yesterday. She was knocking on your door like crazy. When I came out to let her know I could leave a message, she was gone. I assume you heard from her?” 

 

Agatha tapped her fingers along the door handle, hip and head tilted in sync as she stared confused out of her mind. 

 

“What did she look like?” 

 

“Oh, beautiful thing” Sharon smiled. “Dark hair, about your hei-”

 

Rio. 

 

No, that was impossible. Why would she be at her door? And-

 

No. That-

 

Agatha reached up to the top of her doorframe, fingers skimming to make sure the key was actually gone. All that was collected with a dead spider and dust. 

 

Her heart dropped, but sky rocketed at the same time. She felt her mind spiraling out of control. Rio knew where the spare key was, she was at her door and-

 

“Is all okay?” Sharon asked. 

 

Agatha could only force out a pathetic laugh. 

 

“I think I did hear her make it into your apart-”

 

Holy shit. 

 

“Are you serious?” 

 

“Well, you know how thin these walls are. And really you and I are the only two that live here besides all the way down the other end” 

 

She fucking broke in. 

 

Agatha laughed harder this time. This was unbelievable.

 

Rio was the reason her spare key was gone. 

Rio broke into her apartment. 

 

Rio was crazier than she was. Go figure.

 

“Are you alrig-”

 

"Uh, yeah. Yes” Agatha nodded as she started to rush past her.

 

She wasn't going to be a coward in her home, sulk into her lonesome. Not a chance. Agatha was already having a field day in her mind with what she could say. 

 

“Is it often you break into people's apartments? Or am I just a lucky woman?” 

 

“Did you have fun in my place?” 

 

“Care to return my key?” 

 

Oh, there were an endless amount of ways she could confront her. Agatha was already grinning ear to ear in disbelief. 

 

As the older woman went to say something else, Agatha waved over her shoulder while opening the staircase door. Not bothering to wait for an elevator. 

 

“Thank you Mrs Hart!”

 

The door was closing while Agatha's footsteps were racing down the stairs. Not hearing behind her the strong,

 

"It's Sharon!"

 

She was giddy as all hell, too busy to care about anything else. Which only left her to take a small pause that lasted a few seconds. 

 

I'm excited a woman broke into my apartment…

What is wrong with me? 

 

Don't open that door. 

 

It was fine. Who cared Rio was fucking insane? Agatha liked her women crazy at times. And there was something that made her feel warm inside knowing Rio wasn't just able to ignore her again. 

 

But as Agatha tossed her bag and wine in the car, jumped into the driver's seat and started her car up. She did wonder one thing to herself the most…

 

Why did she break in to begin with?

It felt foreign to knock on Rio's door. The place she had almost called her forever home, planned a future for herself to be in. Everything had happened so fast, her head still spun and nearly flew off her shoulders. 

 

For now though, Agatha took a step back while her hips swayed side to side. Lips pursed, foot tapping impatiently. 

 

After a few seconds, Agatha raised her fist to knock again just as the door opened to a sight Agatha had missed dearly. Not just Rio, but it wasn't Professor Vidal from work. 

 

Rio was back to her usual self. The baggy hoodie, loose pair of flannel boxers she always had to pull up on her hips, refusing to get a smaller pair. Her hair was messy, eyes tired. 

 

And yet, Agatha still thought she was the most beautiful thing in the world.

 

Agatha smirked, the rush of humor and joy taking over her. Rio broke into her apartment and holy hell- Agatha was ready to have some fun with that. 

 

"Well. Hiya’ there toot-”

 

SLAM! 

 

Agatha jumped as the heavy door almost broke off the hinges. The loud click of the metal lock being turned. 

 

And really, Agatha should take that as a sign to leave. However, was she ever the type of woman to do what should be done? 

 

Besides, Rio broke into her fucking apartment. How could Agatha just walk away and let this go? 

 

She huffed, stepping off the porch and eyeing the backyard gate. Her shoulders raised, head shook as she stormed over, muttering under her breath, 

 

"Think you're the only one who can break into places? Well-" 

 

She grabbed the handle, but unsurprisingly it was locked. Agatha grumbled a few curse words before looking up and debating the idiotic decision. 

 

Fuck it. 

 

"Let's see how you like when someone breaks in” 

 

With that, Agatha grabbed the top of the wooden fence and pulled herself up. She wasn't the strongest woman, but enough to (while struggling, mind you) swing her one leg over. 

 

She still was muttering under her breath while doing so. And if any neighbor was on their porch, walking by, able to see what was going on? She didn't care to look insane. 

 

“Fucking Rio. Think- ugh! You can, jesus- Be the one to break in. Well, you've got another thing comin-”
