Just as Agatha was bringing her other leg over, her balance was ripped away. The edge of the wooden fence dug into her palms, a sliver certainly making it's way into her skin. 

 

The pain made her jump, legs wobbling as her body decided to go against her. And before she knew it? 

 

“SHIT!”

 

Agatha's body collapsed on the grass (That was definitely not soft to the touch). Her body ached instantly, her heel on the bottom of her boot broke off. However, the pain, shock of the fall. Those weren't her main worries. 

 

Before she knew it, she heard the rough bark while paws raced from the house down to the yard. Agatha winced, hid herself worried Nicky would attack thinking she was an intruder. However, she heard a whimper instead. 

 

He instantly started to sniff her up and down, tail wagging as he greeted her like a long lost friend. (As if they didn't just see each other days ago). 

 

Though the relief over how Nicky remembered her, wasn't going into attack protector mode was very short lived. 

 

"Nicky, wha- Oh..” Rio forced a low laugh, shaking her head. “You have got to be kidding me"

 

Shit.

 

She stormed over, snapping her fingers with a sharp, 

 

"Nicky, get in the house and you!"

 

Nicky whimpered again as he ran back inside. Rio was glaring as she stormed over, ready to kick Agatha physically through the wooden gate door. 

 

Agatha nodded, knowing she went too far. Even if it was only fair Rio broke into her place. This wasn't the safest idea and like always, Agatha acted on impulse without ever thinking things through. 

 

Though, things took a turn as Agatha went to push herself up. She was about to stand on her feet when a strong hiss inflated her lungs, her body gave out to drop back in the dirt and grass below. 

 

Rio laughed in disbelief, shaking her head. 

 

"Oh no, nope” She said. “Don't play the I'm hurt act with me, Agatha. Get the hell out"

 

Agatha nervously laughed, unable to say anything. How was she going to explain this? Billy was the one she'd have to call to pick her up. That'd force her to explain while sitting in urgent care why she broke into Professor Vidal's lawn. 

 

“Agatha!”

 

“I am trying here!” Agatha yelled back. “You could give a woman some grace here for trying”

 

“Grace?!” Rio laughed. “Are you insane?! Jumping over my fence?! Did the door slam in the face not mean shit to you?!"

 

Agatha laughed. The irony was absolutely deadly in that moment to her. 

 

"It isnt funny, Ag-'

 

Fuck. Agatha was this far in. Her ankle certainly busted, death warrant signed, a possible break in charge ahead of her. 

 

Agatha had to remember and act on the reason she was even in this predicament in the first place. 

 

She cleared her throat, forced a calm smile while her hand raised in the air. 

 

"May I have my spare key that sits on my doorframe, please?"

 

Rio was about to yell again when Agatha watched the life drain out of her. And if there were any doubts, misconceptions or mistakes how Rio broke into her apartment? 

 

She fucking did.

 

Agatha grinned and Rio felt her life flash before her eyes. 

 

"Busted, disgusted, never to be trusted" Agatha weakly sang the rhyme.

 

Tongue in cheek, fists clenched into tight balls of fury- Rio was close to kicking the grass and dirt directly into Agatha's mouth to shut her up. 

 

"Look who's talking” Rio muttered, nodding to the gate with a stronger, “Now get off your ass and get walking"

 

"Awe, honey! We're both poets and we don't even know it" Agatha smiled wide, irritating every nerve in Rio's body. 

 

Fucks sake. How did I ever even like her at all? 

 

"Agatha-"

 

“Wait, wait, wait, waitwait, wait, wait!" Agatha held her hand up. "Before you call the cops-"

 

"Too easy" Rio laughed. "Much rather kick you out myself"

 

“Oh good, I don't want to press charges either. That'd be an awkward day in court for us. Can you imagine?” 

 

It was astonishing to Rio how quick Agatha was able to slip back into her annoying, irritating, aggravating self. Even through her obvious physical pain, how she was balling her fists and holding tears back. 

 

If Rio wasn't so angry, she'd be impressed. 

 

“That judge would have a field day with us. Two psychotic women breaking into each other's homes. Oh, it'd be one for the books” 

 

“Get out”

 

“But honey-”

 

“Stop calling me that” 

 

“Fine. Sweetheart-”

 

“Agatha. I swear-”

 

“Swear to break in again? Swear to be break in partnership? Who's turn is it next? Do we break into each other's classrooms? Cars or-”

 

“Agatha! Enough! You shouldn't even be here” 

 

“Mmm, not something expected from a woman who broke into my apart-”

 

“You know what?!” Rio yelled.

 

The woman stormed back inside, leaving Agatha alone to wonder if she was locking her out again. Which was fine. Agatha's hand moved to grab her phone, but-

 

Shit. 

 

Her phone was in the car. She was trapped in Rio's yard on the grass. Most likely locked out, left to be outside for the entire night. 

 

Huh. Never been in this situation before. One for the books.. Agatha thought to herself. 

 

Though, Rio came flying back out as soon as she left. Agatha looked back over with a sigh of relief. 

 

“Oh good, you aren't leaving me here to- Whatthe?!”

 

The edge of a photo nearly clipped Agatha's chin. It dropped on her chest, a suicide bomb Agatha never expected. Though when she flipped the image over-

 

Billy..

 

Suddenly the young man wasn't seen as a hero to pick her up from Rio's yard. But more so the villain she was plotting a murder for. 

 

“Explain that! You want to fake this injury, break into my house. Explain. That!” 

 

The photo was of herself laughing with the date Billy had set her up with. Well, attempted to. It didn't turn out like that at all. However, the photo couldn't show that. 

 

Agatha pushed back up on her elbow, shaking her head frantically as the humor she was holding onto drained from her completely. 

 

"No, no" She rushed. "Rio, that's not-"

 

"Laughing it up with her all while I'm back here freaking out-"

 

"Freaking out is an understatement" Agatha muttered.

 

Bad move. 

 

"Really?!" Rio exclaimed.

 

"Shit, sorry- Sorry! Shouldn't have said that, but" Agatha sighed, shaking her head. “To be fair..you really-"

 

"Are an asshole? Yeah. You are. I'm well fucking aware"

 

Agatha sighed, holding the photo in the air. "Well you're unaware of this. You've got the story wrong"

 

“Oh, do I?” Rio asked. Arms crossed tight, head tilted as she aggressively nodded. “Tell me then. What's the story because this looks like you on a fun little date” 

 

Agatha laughed, but Rio wasn't finding anything about this funny. Another bad move, but Agatha quickly pushed it off. 

 

“We weren't on a date. She was the only woman my age there and I was telling her as well about Billy being pulled over for speed-”

 

“HA!” Rio cackled. “That's a fucking lie!” 

 

“It isn't!”

 

"Billy getting pulled over? Really, Agatha? He is just learning how to curse lately"

 

Agatha laughed, shaking her head violently as she pushed to sit up off her elbows. A hand running through her hair as she tossed the photo to Rio's feet. 

 

“I'm not lying. Yes, Billy set us up on a blind dat-”

 

“That you agreed to?" 

 

“ Blind , Rio. I had no idea” Agatha said. “She didn't want to be on it either and I spent the rest of the trip basically hiding on the couch” 

 

“Mhm, sure. Is that why you couldn't answer me at all? I thought you were busy” 

 

“I-”

 

“You know what? Save it, Agatha. Just get out. I don't care if your ankle, foot, whatever your issue is hurts. Just, get out!”

 

Agatha looked down, hand rubbing over her face as she nodded. Rio went to walk away, turn and not watch Agatha leave. 

 

“Fuck” Agatha gasped as her body collapsed back down. 

 

Shit. 

 

Rio hated herself. Agatha was clearly hurt, unable to hold herself up and she didn't know how to not help her. 

 

She should help her to her car. Either call someone to pick her up or force her to drive herself out of here. 

 

However when Agatha tried to push herself up again and failed- Rio couldn't do it. She couldn't let Agatha go home alone. The woman knew damn well she wouldn't go to urgent care on her own. Billy would most likely take her, but only if Agatha didn't scare him into letting her go home. 

 

Then what? She was on her own, risking a worse injury and- 

 

Fucking hell, I shouldn't care.

 

Rio did though. She cared way too fucking hard. 

 

“Jesus..” She muttered before charging over. 

 

Agatha looked up, showing a bit of panic as she rushed the words- 

 

“I'm trying here, alri- RIO!”

 

Rio wasted no time to loop one arm under her legs, the other supporting her back as she scooped her off the grass. Agatha's arms were quick to wrap around her neck, holding on tight as if Rio would let her fall. 

 

She never would let her fall. Ever. 

 

The younger woman knew Rio hit up the gym a few times a week. She'd nearly manhandle her in bed at times. But being carried like so? Maybe it was the small time apart or just the fact Agatha still found Rio to be the hottest thing on earth. 

 

Holy fuck. Agatha could drool over this alone. 

 

Nicky jumped from his small bed in the living room as the two entered. Agatha was about to say something when Rio dropped her onto the couch, not letting her gracefully sit. 

 

Better than the grass, I guess…

 

Nicky jumped up on the couch next to her. Panting with his tongue out to the side, tail wagging like he was his own helicopter. Agatha couldn't help but focus on him for a few seconds. Too busy ruffling his hair, whispering a small greeting to notice Rio lifting her leg up. Only when it dropped on the pillow did she hiss, whipping her head over. 

 

"Could've been a bit more gracious with the drop here” 

 

"You're lucky I'm not leaving you outside to rot" Rio muttered. "I should, by the way”

 

Rio began working on untying the boot. She didn't look up at Agatha. Focused on making sure her ankle was elevated, careful to not apply pressure as she undid the laces. 

 

Agatha held Nicky close as she watched, stunned by the change of events. 

 

Rio was crouched down, lips pulled back as she handled her with care. From the aggressive greeting, rough handling to carry her inside, swiftly becoming the softest version of a caretaker Agatha had ever seen before. 

 

Not even a nurse in a hospital would be treating her with this level of kindness. 

 

The boot slipped off. Agatha hissed and held onto Nicky tighter. She swore she heard Rio mumble a few apologies, but didn't press on her to admit they were there. 

 

Rio put her shoe aside, looked up with silent eyes that warned Agatha her sock was next. She didn't nod, but there was an understanding between them both. 

 

Her eyes then turned back, pushing her pant leg up to the mid part of her shin. Agatha hated the goosebumps that visibly showed. How Rio's fingers were cold to the touch, yet set her skin on fire from a simple touch. 

 

The pain distracted her from any pinch of arousal. Agatha was silently thankful for that. Though her heart sank as the sock slipped off. Swollen, a shade of a dark bruise already forming at a slow pace. 

 

Though what scared her was the fact it was immediate. Only a few minutes ago did she fall and her ankle already looked busted. She hated urgent care, hospitals, doctors, any medical environment of the sorts. 

 

Agatha was already shaking her head. “It's fine” 

 

Rio hummed. “I don't think-”

 

“No! It's fine” 

 

The older woman looked up from her ankle, meeting the panicked filled eyes staring wide at it. At that moment, Rio didn't see the smug, annoying, cocky woman from before. 

 

This was Agatha. The vulnerable version Rio had access to. The woman she had grown to love, care for, and even through her anger and pain..

 

“Hey,” Rio placed her hand on Agatha's leg, thumb drawing soothing circles. “We don't have to go anywhere” 

 

Agatha met her eyes. Rio's heart broke at the sight of unshed tears, a wall of them built but held at bay. Her bottom lip was quivering, cheeks pale in a sudden flush of sickness.

 

“I think this is just a sprain, really,” Rio said. “Wanda used to get them all the time. Never really needed urgent care or anything” 

 

Agatha swallowed the lump in her throat, wiping under her eyes quick to make sure no tears rolled down her cheeks. She cleared her throat, pushed her shoulder blades back with a shake of her head. 

 

“What makes you so sure?” 

 

Sometimes, it was crazy to Rio how versatile Agatha was. One second her voice was small, the next she was back to her rough attitude filled self. It was impressive to say the least. Though if Rio were Agatha, she'd be exhausted at the constant switch. 

 

Rio pushed up from the floor, stuffing Agatha's sock in her boot before putting it aside. She then moved to bring Agatha's other leg up to rest on the coffee table as well, working on untying it. 

 

“You're not some doctor” 

 

“So, you want to go see one?” Rio asked, looking up at her. “We can get your shoe back on and head out” 

 

Agatha hid a bit in her spot, shaking her head. 

 

“Then why are you questioning me?” 

 

“Why are you being nice to me?” 

 

Rio squinted her eyes, trying to figure out what Agatha's motive was right then. Did she not want to be here? Should Rio call Billy to come get her? 

 

She sighed. Agatha was in pain. Rio had to remember the woman when anxious was a lightswitch that flipped back and forth. One day, she'd look into why that was. The science behind it, maybe pick at her personality a bit more. 

 

But for now, Rio had to focus on her. Make sure she was safe and knew Rio wasn't out to harm her. 

 

“Unfortunately, I don't hate you” Rio said. “Now, can I continue with untying your shoe or do we call an ambulan-”

 

“No” Agatha said in a panicked tone, but then settled with a shrug as if she wanted to appear fearless. “Continue” 

 

Rio hummed, focusing back on her shoe again. 

 

This time it was silent between them. Rio handled her with care while Nicky snuggled into Agatha's side as if he could sense her fear. 

 

Which, Rio knew he most likely could. The boy was always her emotional support. Unsurprisingly, he'd be the same for Agatha as well. 

 

Her shoes were put aside while Rio made sure once again her ankle was properly elevated. 

 

“Ice and painkillers are your friends tonight” Rio said. 

 

“Woo-hoo” Agatha muttered. 

 

Rio couldn't hide the amused smirk on her face, but luckily Agatha didn't see it. She was glaring at her ankle, clearly stuck in her head. 

 

And as soft as Rio was treating her? She couldn't refrain or hold back the comment- 

 

“Well, if you didn't jump my fen-”

 

“You broke into my place first” Agatha snapped her eyes up at her. 

 

Rio snickered. “Didn't have to jump your fence though” 

 

“You still!-” 

 

Agatha went to argue back, but it was Rio who started laughing. The younger woman glared, head tilted as she felt anger rush through her. 

 

“I know you're playing caretaker right now, but you laughing at this is pretty low” 

 

Rio shrugged. “I mean, it's deserved. The whole lie about Billy-”

 

“It isn't a fucking lie!” 

 

“Regardless!” Rio exclaimed. “Do you not hear us right now?” 

 

Agatha fell silent, eyes squinted as she tried to figure out what the woman was saying. Maybe if her ankle wasn't throbbing and anxiety skyrocketing, she'd be able to keep up. But instead, she was at a loss for words. 

 

“What are you talking about?” 

 

Rio rolled her eyes, shaking her head. 

 

“We broke into each other's apartments, Agatha” She said. “And we're bickering over that. This is… insane ” 

 

Agatha took a second to think it over. Logically, she knew this was crazy. They were both out of their ever living, fucking minds. She'd dated some lunatic, off the wall, questionable women in the past. Had been a psychotic ex herself. 

 

But this? Agatha snorted. 

 

“You did it first” She mumbled. “And you still have the key as evidence-”

 

“At least I can still stand on two feet” 

 

Agatha looked up with an amused smile. Her reply was cool, swift and filled with humor. 

 

“Are you saying you're a better criminal than me?” 

 

Rio shrugged. “Intruder is the correct term” 

 

“Oh, so the science professor is trying to correct me? Of all people?” 

 

“Am I wrong?” Rio asked. “You are the one who focuses on partying in the classroom rather than learning” 

 

“Oh here we go again!” Agatha rolled her eyes with a laugh. “Your classroom is not a sacred place for church or a courtroom. All serious and boring-”

 

“I guess I'll just have to break into yours to fix the nightclub, party warehouse atmosphere” 

 

“Oh and who says residence break in talent equals classroom abilities as well?” 

 

“Did you just call me talented?” 

 

They stared at each other with a little bit of glimmer in their eyes. Both smiling and even if they were small grins…they were visible. Seen by the other and made aching hearts swell again. 

 

The two may have been at odds, in a fight, at each other's throats and wondering if this was all the end. But at that moment, something shifted. The air wasn't as thin. Tensions weren't running as high and life threatening. 

 

There was hope in the dark tunnel both had found themselves in. Between Rio not letting Agatha go home alone, being able to still joke and poke fun at each other. 

 

The love was there. It was a bit buried, still had to be uncovered and rebuilt. Yet, both of them felt shivers down their spine. Agatha had to look away to hide the red flush in her cheeks while Rio's tongue swiped the inside of her cheek, looking around the room with a small shake of her head. 

 

Snapping Agatha out of the soft moment was another wince. Rio's head snapped over the second she heard it. Agatha had shifted her ankle on the pillow. Most likely forgetting she had injured it for a moment.

 

Rio held her breath for a second before asking a soft, yet stern,

 

“Think you can manage to sit and keep quiet while I grab you, your new friends?” 

 

Agatha huffed, looking up with a forced grin. Rio could see the pain and how Agatha tried to hide it.

 

“Do I even get a sticker for being so brave?” 

 

“No, you get a get out of jail free card-”

 

“You broke into my place first!” 

 

“And you have no evidence of that” Rio grinned. 

 

“You hold the key and I have an eye witness” 

 

“Your eye witness is an old woman and for all you know, I flushed the key” 

 

“Mrs Hart is a sane woman! Unlike you ” 

 

“Okay, sprained ankle. Whatever you need to tell yourself” 

 

Agatha groaned, head tossed back as Rio left the room laughing. 

 

“I hate you!” 

 

“All the ladies jump over my fence when they hate me!” 

 

“All the crazy bitches break into my apartment!” 

 

Agatha felt her heart swell as Rio's laugh echoed through the house. She turned back around, looking down at Nicky who had his head asleep in her lap. Her fingers traced over his ears, down his back. 

 

She leaned close to his ears, whispering a gentle, 

 

“I don't think your mama hates me. Do you?” 

 

He snored, Agatha grinned. That was enough for her to nod and add a small, 

 

“Agreed” 

 

Maybe there's hope after all…



Slow and Steady Wins the Race

Chapter Notes

Another chapter that didn't take weeks to update oh my god I KNOW ANYWAYYYYY- Hehe. That's all. Just..hehe for this chapter:)) ENJOY

Also if there's any fuck ups I missed in this chapter, Ao3 has been giving me HELL formatting/posting lately:/

"How can we go back to being friends
When we just shared a bed?"

“Go on, buddy” 

 

Agatha heard the soft voice drift through from the kitchen. The smell of strong coffee followed, waking her up more than she was before. It took a few seconds for the woman to remember where she was. The familiar living room, comfortable atmosphere, Rio's voice and Nicky's paws tapping against the floorboards. 

 

The realization should freak her out. Snap her awake, strike fear into her. Though, none of that existed. Agatha was too busy trying to remember when a fleece blanket covered her body. She couldn't recall falling asleep either. 

 

None of that mattered the second the instant ache, throbbing sensation came out of its own slumber as well. Agatha hissed, readjusting on the couch with her eyes squeezed shut. 

 

“Shit, shit” She whispered to herself. 

 

Right, her ankle. Agatha almost forgot that was the entire reason Rio had allowed her to stay the night. More so, didn't give her a choice. Not that Agatha had any complaints. 

 

She managed to move her legs off the couch, pushing herself to sit upright with another painful, suffocated whimper. Careful to not alert Rio in the next room. Agatha already knew the lecture she'd get for mov-

 

Wait till she leaves. Agatha quickly thought to herself. 

 

Rio would be frantic, overbearing, suffocating her if Agatha dared to walk to the bathroom on her own. Agatha knew she meant no harm, but after last night? The grogginess, pain, she felt that second? Agatha didn't need someone breathing down her neck. 

 

She checked the time on her phone, seeing Rio was due to walk out the door in the next twenty minutes. 

 

I can wait. Agatha told herself. 

 

Like clockwork, footsteps entered the living room from the kitchen. Agatha looked up to see Rio as her Professor Vidal self. No more baggy hoodie and boxers. Now clean, put together in a-

 

“New outfit?” Agatha asked. 

 

Rio jumped, looking over her shoulder as she reached for her boots. 

 

Agatha had to swallow the lump in her throat, refraining herself from drooling on the spot. Rio looked frighteningly good. 

 

From the tight pair of black pants that clung to her hips, legs, all the right places. A dark green shirt with the sleeves rolled up. The top three buttons undone. 

 

Her hair was held back in a hair clip, makeup dark to bring the brown orbs to life. 

 

“What about it?” Rio asked. 

 

Agatha's mouth was dry, lips parted as her brain malfunctioned. This was typical when Rio strutted down the halls. The times Agatha could see through her door how she ruled a classroom. Hand in the air, the other in her pocket while walking around. 

 

And yet? Agatha felt more stupid than she was before. 

 

“Uh,” Agatha cleared her throat, shaking her head. “Nothing..” 

 

Before Rio could push or tease her on it, Agatha went to move- Instantly hissing a strong, 

 

“Shit! Shit-”

 

“Easy” Rio dropped her boots, rushing over to help. 

 

She lifted Agatha's leg gently to return it to the same pillow from the night before. Propped up on the coffee table, elevated perfectly. 

 

“Not any better today, I take it?” Rio asked. 

 

Agatha scoffed. “How could you tell? Idiot..” 

 

Rio smirked as she pulled Agatha's pant leg up, checking the damage to see it a darker shade of purple- nearly a dark gray or black. It was swollen, a sprain stronger than Rio ever managed to have. 

 

“You sure I just sprained it?” Agatha asked. “Not a break?”

 

Rio huffed a little laugh, but Agatha didn't react. Her eyes were glued on the injury. The pair nearly bulged out of their socket, clearly scared and fearing the worst. 

 

She softened, rolling the cuff of Agatha's pant leg to keep it above. Just enough so when Rio returned with the ice pack, it could sit below it. 

 

“No, it's a sprain. I told you that last nigh-”

 

“But what if you're wrong?” Agatha asked. 

 

Her tone was filled with attitude, but Rio didn't take it personal. She sighed, hands on her hips with a shrug. 

 

“Do you want to go to the ER to find ou-”

 

“No, I'm sure it's a sprain” Agatha muttered quick, slouching into the couch with her lips pursed in a pout.

 

Rio hinted at a smile, struggling to hide it. Agatha was adorable. In pain, but still cute. Especially because Rio knew she'd never show this vulnerable, scared side of herself to anyone else. 

 

After everything the last week or so had brought on- Rio still had access to the real Agatha Harkness. 

 

“Like I said, Wanda had them all the time. Twisted, sprained, all her forte” Rio shrugged. 

 

Agatha chuckled. That familiar light switch of a personality flickered again. Vulnerable to humorous in just a quick beat. Rio always wondered why that was. How she was that way. 

 

Agatha was a wonder of things to Rio, but more so a mystery case she'd never get tired of finding the pieces to. Another reason Rio was so addicted. Not only her love, but intrigue as well remained strong. 

 

“Is that why she's gay then?” Agatha asked.

 

Rio paused, head tilted with an eye roll. “What? No, it doesn't work like tha-”

 

“Do you think each time she twisted it- Her sexuality went from straight to gay, straight to gay, and she just landed on gay?” 

 

Agatha's hand had flicked left to right each time she said ‘straight to gay’ . Then right after, she looked up with an innocent face matching a tiny grin. Yet still able to look serious as can be. 

 

Rio took in a deep breath, forcing herself to shake her head while bringing her hand over her mouth- hiding the little smile. 

 

“You're so fucking stupid” Rio muttered. 

 

Agatha laughed. This time a louder one, but it still sounded exhausted. Rio found herself wondering how Agatha slept. 

 

Did the pain keep her up all night? Was she uncomfortable? Had Rio made the right decision by keeping her there for the night? 

 

Her laugh cut short, hiding behind the back of her hand- Eyes squeezed shut had betrayed trying to hide the next wave of pain that seethed through her. 

 

“I'll be right back. Getting you some pain meds and an ice pack”

 

“Oh yay, my friends” Agatha cheered in a monotone voice. 

 

Rio rolled her eyes, making her way back to the kitchen. Nicky walked through the backdoor, not stopping as he bolted for the living room. 

 

“Easy with her Nick-”

 

“OOF!” Agatha groaned with a laugh that settled Rio's fear. “Good morning, baby boy” 

 

Agatha greeted in a warm voice. No longer sounded in pain, teasing tone, none of it. And as Rio popped the bottle of Tylenol open, she couldn't ignore the swelling ache in her chest. 

 

Her mornings had been quiet, too silent for her liking. Even with an energetic dog like Nicky. This only made Rio realize what she already knew, but confirmed it. 

 

Agatha was her noise. 

 

She missed hearing the two have their tiny morning talks. Rio missed when Agatha would hum in the morning or be grumpy and complain it was too early to be up. She missed Agatha taking up half her space, bickering over the bathroom, being in the way and-

 

Fuck. Rio missed Agatha ( Duh ). 

 

Rio grabbed the ice pack, wrapping it in a hand towel before bringing them back to Agatha. 

 

The exchange was silent between them. Agatha took the two pills, grabbing her water bottle from her side. Rio crouched down, gently placing the ice pack over her ankle- Whispering soft apologies as Agatha hissed. 

 

“Too cold?” Rio asked. 

 

Agatha shook her head. Rio nodded, pushing back up with a sigh. 

 

The moment was silent as Rio moved to grab the TV remote, her laptop and a charger for it. Agatha gave her a questioning look, but was able to answer Rio's stare without needing to hear it. 

 

“Lilia will-”

 

“I'm moving my classes online right now” Agatha grumbled as she opened her emails to do so. “So bossy..” 

 

“Saving your ass from the wrath of Lilia? Oh, I know. Poor you, my love” 

 

The little name rolled off her tongue before she could catch it. Both froze, but Rio ran away from the moment before it became anything else. 

 

She slipped on her boots, making sure her bag and keys were together. 

 

“I'll leave the backdoor open for Nicky” Rio said, making her way to the kitchen to grab her coffee. 

 

Now, Rio made it clear to herself when she started the coffee machine that morning- 

 

Only coffee for me. 

 

It was petty, but Rio was struggling to not easily cave back into Agatha's arms. By making Agatha coffee, she was catering to her completely. Not just being a caretaker with medication and a place to heal. That'd be luxury and-

 

I'm not doing that. 

 

Rio walked back in the living room, taking a show filled sip from the travel mug to try and brag. 

 

That's where she fucked up. 

 

Agatha's blue eyes turned from an annoyed stare into puppy ones. Where she was silently begging for coffee. Rio wondered if her hopes were up at the smell of it. 

 

Nope. No. Don't give in.

Fuck.

She's mine.

“You're so fucking annoying”

Thank fuck. She ordered food.

Right. Shit.

What if she was seriously hurt and I got back too late?

An unspoken bond had been formed. One fueled by love that couldn’t slip away that easy. And maybe that’s what freaked Rio out the most. How one moment she was on her own. She didn’t need a lover, another person in her life. 

 

Sure, it had gotten lonely. However, she was safe. No harm or fears on the horizon. But now? 

 

As Rio moved to sit on the edge of the bathtub, back resting against the wall, not caring if the humidity would make the back of her shirt damp. Her eyes peaked up to see Agatha on the other end. She was finishing off the last bite of her crust. Eyes closed, peaceful. 

The water line was just under her collarbone. Hair untouched, but droplets of water trickled down her neck. It stunned Rio how beautiful Agatha was. This hadn’t been the first time she noticed, but again- It was different.

 

“What if we rushed into this?” Rio blurted. 

 

The question whispered in one breath had rolled off her tongue, taking herself by surprise. She felt guilt suffocate her as the blue eyes snapped open, worrisome and struck with a sense of doom. 


Rio didn’t want and hadn’t meant to do that to her. But, she couldn’t control or refrain from asking. 

 

Was it to protect herself? Make Agatha question everything about them as well? The younger professor seemed so confident constantly. Little blips of vulnerability slipped through the cracks of her tough exterior. Yet, she stood tall and Rio somewhat envied it. 

 

“Into what?” Agatha asked. 

 

There it was. The little secret of her sensitive side shining bright. Rio had done that. She brought it out of her and the woman had a love/hate relationship with how she held the ability to do so. 

 

They were too far in for Rio to backtrack, peddle, reverse and drive herself off the cliff from this. Agatha wouldn’t let her run off. Even if she had a brutally sprained ankle, Agatha would follow and take every fall to catch Rio- force the topic of discussion out of her. 


Rio cleared her throat, shrugging as she looked down. 

 

“Us. This” She said. “I mean, I hated you for years” 

 

Agatha snorted. “You thought I was hot though” 

 

Rio looked back up, eyes that told Agatha she was serious. The smirk her lover wore only lasted a few seconds after that. 

 

“Don’t be so smug” 

 

As her smirk faded, Agatha whispered a soft, fear filled question herself,

 

“What are you saying?”

 

“I-”

 

“Do you regret the last few months then?” 

 

“No” 

 

Her answer was short, fast. As if it was a reflex, knee jerk reaction. 

 

The comfortable tension started to tighten. A rubber band being pulled, threatening to snap at any given moment. Rio started to hate it. A sinking feeling in the pit of her stomach. Her chest was clenching. Suddenly the humid room felt too small for two. 

 

Rio shook her head, going to stand as she mumbled a low,

 

“Forget it”

 

“No,” Agatha copied the same answer as Rio seconds prior. She held her hand out, eyes glaring, “Sit” 

 

“Ag-”

 

“If you dare leave this room, I will follow” She warned. “Pain and all, you’re not leaving”

 

Rio subtly smiled in her mind. Not over the threat, but how she predicated Agatha’s reaction perfectly. With the idea of her falling, injuring herself more- Rio relaxed in her spot the best she could. A posture that told Agatha she wasn’t going anywhere. 

 

Agatha coughed a low, ahem, earning Rio’s attention. Her fingers wiggled, pointing at the wine bottle. Rio quickly opened the cap for her before passing it over. She watched as Agatha took a generous sip, letting the rim of the bottle rest on her lips for a few seconds- Taking the second swig with a nod. 

 

“K’..” 

 

She whispered, putting the bottle on the floor before running hands through her hair. Agatha tapped her fingers against the base of her skull, scrunching her nose, tilting her head side to side before sitting taller. 

 

And then, she tossed in the air between them a fast sentence. One rushed as if she worried herself she’d fail to get the words out. 

 

“As much as we both hate it- We have to talk…so-”


She reached down again, grabbing the bottle of wine and held it up for Rio to take. A forced smirk, yet relaxed at the same time. Rio could read the fear and hesitation behind it. 

 

“Liquid courage, baby” She rasped. 

 

Fuck. Rio adored her. How could she not?

 

The way her voice was hoarse, tone low. A sexy rasp that’d never fail to send chills down her spine. It reminded her of early mornings. When Agatha was groggy, rubbing her eyes and mumbling complaints. For the grump she was, Rio felt far too fond of that and missed easy, blissful moments like those. 

 

Rio rolled her eyes. Not only at Agatha, but herself. She shouldn’t be scared of this. The woman was a fucking adult for crying out loud and being in love still scared her?

 

Pathetic.

 

She took the bottle of wine, raising it to take a lingering sip herself. A little rush ran through her at the realization hitting her. 

 

Agatha’s lips were just- 

 

Rio jerked the bottle away, not focusing on if it was obvious or not. She put it back on the sink counter, picking at the hangnail off her thumb right after. 

 

The quiet didn’t last as long as she hoped for. Agatha was impatient, quick to push buttons and didn’t think through her words like Rio would. 


A blessing and a curse. 

 

“Did you really hate me? Do you still?” Agatha asked.


“I don’t..” Rio whispered, but then pulled her lips back with a subtle shrug. “But..I thought I did” She whispered. “I mean, you annoyed the shit out of me. Still do” 

 

Agatha hinted a little smirk. “But you like it”

 

“You’re so full of yourself” Rio rolled her eyes. Her voice warm enough to soften the tension. 

 

“And you like that too” Agatha smiled. “But..continue”

 

Rio then had the floor, but for what exactly? To go into more detail how she hated her? Or, question if this was all worth it, possibly rushed. 

 

Her mind drifted to the first part. She remembered how envious, jealous at times in the beginning Rio was of her. Agatha entered the university and became a force to be reckoned with. 

 

She held confidence stronger than anyone Rio had met. Her classes gained popularity higher than what they’d seen before. Everyone fawned over her, wanted to be in her orbit while Rio was on the outskirts questioning everything about her. 

 

The jealousy for her career didn’t last long. Rio was content with her own. She loved her job, students, her classroom was a second home and no one would take that from her. 

 

However, everything else about Agatha was…frightening.

 

Rio was never one to feel an urge to be with the others. She didn’t flock with the sea of birds surrounding the new shiny toy. With Agatha though? Rio stood on her tip toes to get a glimpse from afar. Hidden stares that were poorly disguised as disgusting glares. It became obvious over the years too, Agatha noticed her. 


And maybe that’s what started to scare her more. 

 

Rio’s stares and glares were met with little smirks, fingers wiggled while Agatha would mouth ridiculous flirts. It felt teasing, but not in a romantic way. To Rio, Agatha was taunting her. Making a joke, making fun of her. 

 

Agatha would gift her stupid shit. From that cactus with the note how she was a prick to markers that were ran out of ink with a note, 

 

“You can toss these for me. Thanks!” 

 

It was all juvenile, annoying and didn’t help Rio’s wondering if this was some weird bully. Yes, bully. Even as an adult she wondered. 

 

Old habits die hard..

 

Maybe part of her fear that this was too quick originated from all of those things. Was this a taunt, a long trickful play that would blow up in her face at the end? 

 

“You gave me hell..” Rio whispered. “How could I not hate you?”

 

Agatha held her breath, clearly conflicted with what reply to give. Rio took the floor and continued standing in it, dominating the conversation more. 

 

“The shitty gifts, teasing, it all-”

 

“Was stupid, I know” Agatha nodded, chin propped on her hand while her elbow rested on the edge of the tub. “I just..didn’t know how to get you to pay attention to me” 

 

Rio squinted her eyes. “What?” 

 

Agatha hummed, looking down in disgrace. “It was juvenile. The little tricks and shit, I know”

 

“It was..” Rio agreed. 

 

“And I’m not defending it, but genuinely that was the only way my mind was telling me I could get you to see me” 

 

Agatha looked back up and Rio saw it. The truth covered her from head to toe. No hiding the truthful sincerity, regret and embarrassment behind each word. 

 

“A stupid little crush, really” Agatha forced a little laugh, shaking her head. 

 

Rio stammered, struggling to find the words. “What do- I don’t get it”

 

“What don’t you get?”

 

“What do you mean by my attention?”

Agatha huffed, shaking her head. “Just that. Your attent-”

 

“Was I untouchable or something? Unapproachable or-”

 

“You really don’t get it, do you?” 

 

A few seconds of silence lasted, but Agatha wasn’t able to wait for Rio to reply. She sat up a bit more, head tilted while she rambled on, 

 

“Do you have any idea of how highly you are thought of, Rio?” She asked, not giving her a chance to reply. “So many students talk about how only the smartest ones get into your class. Colleagues admire you, look at you and see you as one of the greats”

 

“Agatha-”

 

“You’re one of a kind. Some kind of rarity that only a few will ever have the honors of meeting in their lifetime” Agatha said. “You gave me a cold shoulder, but apparently that’s common coming from you. However, that couldn’t change what I thought..”

 

Agatha pulled her lips back, biting down on them with a shake of her head as she stared at Rio in disbelief. 

 

“Why on earth would you ever pay attention to a professor like myself?” She asked.

 

Holy shit..

 

While Rio always thought Agatha was cocky, smug, full of herself. Had she seriously been on the sidelines with this feeling? Did she really believe Rio was someone who looked down on her?

 

All this time while Rio was convinced Agatha judged her..there was more to it.

 

“Did you think I looked down on you?” Rio asked. 

 

Agatha snickered. “It was obvious, wasn’t it? You called my classes pointless parties, disrupting and-”

 

“I don’t understand your teaching style entirely and I probably never will, but..” Rio said. “Let’s be honest here..”

 

She swallowed the nervous lump in her throat, foot tapping against the floor with her knee rapidly bouncing. A tick of her fear bleeding through. 

 

“Why would you ever want to be with the strict, boring, professor?” She asked. “It’d always made more sense to me for you to be with someone…more like you” 

 

Agatha shook her head. A little laugh, but it wasn’t filled with humor. 

 

“You don’t get it” She said. “And you’re not hearing me”

 

“I’m hearing you, but trying to get clarification and my side of it” 

 

“I was infatuated with you from the get go, Rio. Sure, I messed up somewhat and didn’t know how to go about it. But..you were the only professor in that entire building who made sense to me”

 

“How? You called me stuck up, boring, stubborn”

 

“And you never heard me when I complimented how you deeply care about your students, your work and-”


Rio scoffed. “When did you do that?” 

 

“Multiple times. In between insults and-”

 

“Oh, well-” Rio laughed. “Sorry, I was too busy tuning you out-”

 

“Exactly!” Agatha said. “The only way you ever heard me was those insults, shitty gifts, pranks” She said. “I didn’t know how else to get through to you that I wanted you” 

 

Oh..

 

Rio somewhat could recall the start of compliments, but they always turned into a joke. Yet looking back on those times. The look Rio knew now, how she was able to read every page of Agatha..

 

I really did intimidate her…holy shit. 

 

“And Rio? You are not as stuck up as you think” Agatha chuckled. “Maybe you only believe it because you are wildly known as the stubborn one”

 

“Exac-”

 

“Let me finish” Agatha held her hand up to silence her. “That’s you at work, Rio. Your job as much as you may view it does not define who you are” Agatha added. “And as much as I became obsessed with a professor? That’s not who I fell in love with”

 

Fell in love..

 

In love…

 

Rio repeated the words in her mind, spiraling and drowning in them. Her heart started to pound, the fear of Agatha doing all of this out of some joke disappearing. 

 

“But still,” Rio whispered. “I’m stubborn, like you said. Boring, all of it. So why should you be with m-”

 

“You have multiple lego sets hidden in the closet which I can not comprehend because it’d be adorable watching you build those. Your drunken voicemail confessed to hiding dinosaur boxers- Which, by the way? I bought you a few more pairs” 

 

Rio’s eyes widened, the fast pace rambling only picking up speed with every word spoken. 

 

“You have a routine of watching cartoons with your dog. You spoil the hell out of him too and even buy him sweaters and little hats. Don’t think I never notice how you and Wanda have a photoshoot for any new outfit you dress him in. You get giddy when I call you stupid little names. When you’re half asleep, you are the most clingy woman I’ve ever met. You cry at chick flicks, you squeal when you bring home a new plant-”

 

Agatha took a breath, shaking her head as she drunkenly smiled as if listing things about Rio was intoxicating. 

 

“You’re more than just a stuck up fucking stubborn, boring as hell professor, idiot” She whispered. “I barely started, by the way. I could keep going and all this would show is you make fucking sense for me” 

 

Rio’s heart was hammering now. A heart attack begging to happen. No one ever described her that way. Ex lovers barely paid attention to her, let alone everything down to the smallest details. 

 

“You may have spent years thinking that way, but just know I spent years myself thinking you’d never view me as anything but annoying and immature” Agatha smirked. 

 

She shook her head a tiny bit, whispering under her tongue, 

 

“You’re insane, Harkness..” 

 

Agatha shrugged. “You’re an idiot, Vidal” 

 

All of this. The confession, ramble, answers given for why things were said and done. And yet? There was still hesitation on Rio’s end. Agatha seemingly read it for what she added on. 

 

“I waited three years, Rio..” She whispered. “I can wait more. If easing into this is what you need, so be it. I’m more than willing to be your friend”

 

Friends?

 

Rio laughed. “I don’t know how to just be your friend”

 

“Then we don’t have to call this anything” Agatha shrugged. “We’ll take it day by day”

Rio looked down in shame, but Agatha was having none of it. She lowered her hand, splashing a bit of water at the older woman who jumped in response. A little laugh was on Agatha’s end. Especially when a glare was shot her way. 

 

“Stop looking like I kicked your puppy-”

 

“You would never kick Nicky” Rio said, reaching over for the hand towel to try her face. 

 

“And I would never judge you for needing time..” Agatha said. “Maybe I need it as well. Maybe we both do” 

 

Rio finished drying her face, lowering the towel on her lap. She looked up at Agatha, letting out a low sigh before whispering, 

 

“What if you find someone else?” Rio asked. “In the meantime, I-”

 

“Well, I am down for the count right now,” She gently raised her leg, but not enough to kick her ankle out of the water. “Sprained ankle and all. So..I’m not running anywhere” 

 

Rio glared, not amused by the answer. Agatha snickered, finding herself funny as always. 

 

“Rio,” She sighed. “You’ve been on my mind and in my eyesight for years. Unfortunately, that isn’t changing”

 

“Unfortunately..” Rio muttered. 

 

“It’s true” Agatha shrugged. “For all the sexy professors in that building. The toughest, stubborn one had to be my favorite” 

 

Rio squinted her eyes in disgust. “All the sexy professors?”

 

Agatha grinned wide. She sat up, leaning close to Rio without thinking how her chest raised out of the water. Exposing the top part of her breasts. She didn’t miss the flicker of Rio’s eyes down before back up at her. 

 

“Between that and your jealous little tone about other professors? We can manage to be friends and not find anyone else for a bit” 

 

Rio felt her cheeks burn, looking down before away. This time Agatha snorted, finding it funny how Rio struggled poorly to hide her lust. Yet, it was comforting to know that it was still there. Not going anywhere for the time being. 

 

“When did you become so…open?” Rio asked. “I think this is the most emotional speech I ever heard from you..” 

 

Agatha was shocked herself by the downpour of words herself. No one ever gave her the confidence to be this way. She never was able to find the right words, feel safe enough to even breathe them into the open. 

 

But with Rio?

 

“I don’t know..” She shrugged. “I guess disgusting love makes the unthinkable happen”


Rio smirked, shaking her head. “You’re a lunatic, Harkness” 

 

“And you’re the same as me” 

 

“Sometimes” Rio said. 

 

“Now,” Agatha held her hand out. “Pizza me” 

 

“Pizza you?” Rio snickered, opening the box by her side to grab a piece for her. “Would you like me to even feed you grapes, your majesty?”

 

Agatha took the slice from her, taking a bite as she gasped. 

 

“Ooo, ‘oleplay ahead?” She asked, mouthful of food with her words. Eyebrows wiggled and caused a stir of butterflies in Rio’s stomach. “Keep that in mind” She winked. 

 

Rio shook her head. “I really fucking hate you” 

 

“Ditto, toots” 

 

They fell into the same comfortable silence from before once again. Rio took another slice to eat, both passing the wine bottle between them. Nothing needed to be said when it was all out in the open. They’d be friends, maybe not even that. Not labeling what they were felt safer to them both for some reason. 

 

Rio knew one day, she’d do the same for her. The way Agatha gave an emotional, love filled speech- Rio wanted that. Maybe it’d be easier in writing, another lengthy text or voicemail. She’d think about it as time passed. 

 

For now though? She’d focus on gaining trust. Unknowingly, Agatha would have to focus on something herself. She gave an entire saga, ramble, but never told Rio how her walls had never been shattered before. 

 

Agatha would use the time to learn how to feel comfortable with that. The fact Rio had access to her inside and out. Agatha had to come to terms with being a sucker, love drunk fool who would stop the world if Rio asked her to. She needed to be okay before going forward with being this new vulnerable person. Plus, accepting she was someone who could be loved. 

 

It was challenging enough to let Rio care for her. Sit in this bathtub, have someone rage over her stupiud antics from letting a stranger in her car then the house. No one ever cared or questioned Agatha’s impulsive, reckless decisions. No one ever cared if she fell or was sick, injured. 

 

Agatha was always on her own, but that didn’t seem to be her future any longer. Unless she pushed Rio away, Agatha was determined to prevent that at all costs. When before in her life, she’d already be long gone. Agatha would have quit her job, skipped down, ditched Rio aside like she never existed.

 

Things were changing. Maybe for the better, maybe for the worse. But both women knew they couldn’t risk losing whatever it was. Their love, bond, it had taken control and they either had to accept it, learn to work through it- Or, completely give up. 

 

Neither wanted the second.  

 

“Hey Rio..” Agatha broke the silence. 

 

Rio looked up. “Yeah?”

 

Agatha smirked a bit, picking at her food with a tiny shrug. “...You know I used your Zoom account on purpose, right?” 

 

Rio paused, watching the humor light up Agatha like a Christmas tree. Another little antic, prank. One of many that only made Rio shake her head over. 

 

“I mean, I do know how to log out, but..” She shrugged. “I was bored” 

 

Rio faked an annoyed sigh, but shrugged her shoulders in an nonchalant manner. If Agatha wanted to play this game. Two can play at once. 

 

“That's fine..” Rio pushed up. She started to walk out of the bathroom, but then snapped her fingers while whipping around. “That reminds me- Billy knows about us”

 

And with that, Rio watched Agatha’s smirk fade into eyes widened. As much as she loved Rio, spilled the emotional ramble- Rio knew Agatha would stress over someone (Especially Billy) knowing she was a sucker for love.

 

Billy would never shut up or let her live this down either. 

 

“He knows WHAT?!”  

 

Rio laughed, shutting the bathroom door behind her with a grin. The muffled sound through the door only made her laugh harder. 

 

“Get back here, Rio!” 

 

“Be with you in a moment, sweetheart!” 

 

Rio started to put the leftover pizza in a ziplock bag to keep as leftovers. A smile was permanent, giggling as she heard Agatha grumbling curses and threats to kill her. She felt at ease Agatha was willing to go slow, day by day. 

 

But..one question remained. 

 

How can I ever just be her friend?  

 

And in Agatha's mind while she was ready to curse Rio and Billy out both? It was worth the wait. Rio was worth it. Besides, there was the cliche saying,

 

Slow and steady wins the race...

Sweet Thang in the Gardens

Chapter Notes

13k words of tooth rotting sweetness. Enjoy now because upcoming chapters is a bit of a rollercoaster again lol

"Ooh, baby. Sweet thang"

Rio spent the following two weeks with classes online, working from her home office. Agatha argued with her on it a bit, but ultimately wouldn’t deny being in the same house as Rio made her feel better day by day.

 

She worked in the dining room, glasses perched on her nose with her ankle elevated on the opposite chair. Their classes weren’t on the same schedule. So at times, Rio would walk in the kitchen and spot Agatha through the entryway. She’d resist a smile the best she could. See the way the woman was stuck in a chair, but still able to have the most alive presence. 

 

Her hands would be everything, arms flailing while speaking loud. She could hear laughter through the speakers. Her students still attached, hooked on every word and joked along with her. 

 

For the last few years, Rio only heard about Agatha’s classes. The muffled noise, laughter, music that sometimes played too loud for her liking. She never actually saw up close Agatha’s teaching style. Who she was ruling a classroom. 

 

Safe to say for the last few weeks? Rio Vidal was impressed. 

 

She knew Agatha took pride in her work and her students loved her. Rio somewhat had an idea why, but now she knew. She wasn’t a student herself and even if she hadn’t been falling in love with Agatha, she’d be mesmerized. 

 

Agatha was a witch who caught your attention, kept you focused on her and nothing else. Hence why she did catch the university by storm and became one of the favorites. Rio’s favorite thing was how Agatha was able to playfully insult a student while lifting them up at the same time. 

 

“Now! Let’s do a little roleplay. Ryan! Yes you, deer in headlights, half asleep boy in the back with the snore louder than storm in Wisconsin” 

 

The class laughed, but Agatha didn’t let it last long before continuing. 

 

“Give me an improve speech. Any subject your sleepy little heart desires. Three, two, one-” 

 

Rio hadn’t listened to the student. Only focused on Agatha who was taking notes, eyes glued to the screen with a few nods as he spoke. When he started to stammer, pause in between words, Agatha snapped her fingers. 

 

“What happened?” She asked.

 

The young man was stuttering through his reply. Agatha cut him off before he could finish. 

 

“You lost your confidence,” She said. “You let all these little pairs of eyes in tiny boxes on a screen intimidate you and lost sight of the point”

 

“No, don’t be ashamed. No pouting, frowning- What does that God awful dance teacher say? One in the wheelchair, went to prison?” Agatha asked. 

 

A student replied with the name. Agatha snapped her fingers, pointing at the screen. 

 

“Save those tears- You know what? No. I don’t like her. She sounds like a bitch teacher. I’m a nightmare, but not your worst like a convict. Anyway! Besides the point. Ladies because no one likes a man- You MUST never let the others intimidate you” 

 

From that point on, Rio spent her early afternoon lunch grading papers in the kitchen to watch Agatha teach. Only a few times did the younger woman look up, but had to control herself because her cheeks would burn red and she’d struggle to hide how giddy she became. 

 

However, as the first two weeks closed and Rio was due back to campus Monday morning- Agatha called her out on it. 

“No extra audience during my second class of the day” Agatha sighed. “I’ll be bored. Maybe you can put a stand up cardboard of yourself to gaze at me?”

 

Rio scoffed, stirring the pasta on the stove. Agatha sat at the kitchen table behind her. In just a tank top, hair pulled back in a messy bun, glasses falling to the center of her nose. 

 

“I don’t gaze-”

 

“So you stare?”

 

“More so glare”

 

“Now is that anyway to look at a dear friend of yours?”

 

The friend thing, yeah. They could laugh over ​​it. Neither wanted to admit how miserably they were failing at accomplishing that. 

 

Sure, they hadn’t kissed or slept in the same bed. That was because they were frequently falling asleep on the couch. Both blamed it on watching a movie or TV show late into the night. When in reality, neither admitted how they didn’t want to sleep apart from the other. Especially Rio who had been a bit over protective of Agatha. 

 

It didn’t help that Agatha refused to see a doctor. No medical attention for her ankle. Rio hovered over her more because of it and maybe it was a stupid idea? But that was part of the reason Agatha didn’t want to seek help. Not only her fear of any medical environment, but also Rio was constantly around her. 

 

She helped her walk, made her every meal, catered to her and sat in the bathroom with her when Agatha was in the bath (Which was ran by Rio). For two so-called friends, things felt like a domestic relationship between two lovers. 

 

Not surprising in the slightest, but neither did a thing to acknowledge they were not friends at all. 

 

Ultimately, Monday came too soon for Agatha’s liking. Rio’s as well. 

 

The older woman made Agatha a coffee and breakfast. Made sure the pain med schedule was written down, ice packs in the freezer were available. Agatha was luckily better with walking, but still had to take it easy and limit her movement. 

 

Rio was confident she wouldn’t be following that last part since Rio wasn’t home to make her. Which led her to ask Wanda to drop by around noon with lunch, hoping Agatha wouldn’t catch on to Rio being the reason she was there. 

 

Around noon that day, the door opened with a soft, 

 

“Yoo-hoo!” 

 

From the entryway. Nicky ran up, tail wagging with little whimpers of excitement. Agatha had just ended her first class of the day. A three hour one that took up her morning. She jumped over the entrance, leaning back to see Wanda striding through the kitchen with take out food in her hands. 

 

Agatha scoffed, raising her glasses to sit on her head with a little laugh.

 

“What? Did she seriously recruit you to spy on me?”

 

Wanda put the foot down, shaking her head while turning to ruffle Nicky’s fur. 

 

“Maybe I just wanted to see my special boy!” 

 

Agatha rolled her eyes, reaching over to see the food she brought. It was funny to her how unbothered she was from the intrusion. Typically, she didn’t like unannounced entrances. However, there was something about Wanda that didn’t bother her. 

 

And maybe it was related to Rio caring from afar. 

 

“So! How’s the ankle? I’m an expert in this area” 

 

Agatha snickered. “So I’ve heard” 

 

The redhead sat down across the table. The two grabbed their salads. Agatha pushed her laptop to the side, seeing a chicken caesar one for her. 

 

“Yeah, she sent you alright..” Agatha snickered. 

 

There was no way Wanda knew that was her favorite without Rio telling her. Not a chance. 

 

Wanda sighed, giving a little smile. “I’m sorry. Seriously. But, you know how she is..” 

 

Agatha shook her head, taking a bite. She smiled at the taste. A salad from her favorite restaurant. Once again she knew, this is all Rio. 

 

“Don’t worry about it” Agatha said. “I wouldn’t want you to risk your life by going against orders”

 

Wanda chuckled. “It is really insane to us what you’ve done to her” 

 

Agatha furrowed her eyebrows, waiting till she swallowed her food before asking, 

 

“What’s that supposed to mean?”

 

“She’s more open, I’d say. Happier even” Wanda said. “I’ve never seen this Rio in my lifetime”

 

Agatha felt butterflies tickle her stomach, swirling in a cloud of chaos. Her cheeks burned, looking down to hide the red brighter than Wanda’s hair. 

 

“I was hesitant, I’ll admit” Wanda said. “After the little…silence you two had-”

 

“Shit, I swear- That won’t happen again” Agatha assured. 

 

“It better not,” Wanda warned. “I may be nice, but I know how to sprain two ankles and other bones as well” 

 

Agatha stabbed at her food, losing an appetite as guilt swallowed her. The uncomfortable, stomach turning memory played again. Only a few weeks ago had she given Rio nothing but silence. Listened to those heartbreaking voicemails, prepared herself to lose her altogether. 

 

Everything felt like a fever dream, a nightmare that stuck with you for life. One you never were fully able to forget. Wanda must’ve seen the turn in Agatha. She worked quickly to change the subject back to a light hearted one.

“Food”

Is that good?

Is this..did I stress her out?

It’s too much. Fuck.

No one had ever made this sort of grand gesture for Rio. 

 

No one ever loved me like this.

Saturday morning was loud to say the least. At the crack of dawn, Agatha woke up with Nicky under her head. It became a routine how she used him as a pillow and he was more than happy to be that. 


No, Agatha still wasn’t in Rio’s bed. But the couch had grown comfy for her. It was closer to the bathroom and the kitchen combined. So, she couldn’t complain. 


She groaned into his fur as the music played from the kitchen. The smell of coffee filled the air, dishes clinking together with feet shuffling all over the floorboards. 

 

“What is your mother doing?” She asked. 

 

Agatha regretfully got up from the couch. Her walking was a tad bit easier, but still a little unstable. Nicky loved to walk by her side early mornings. Almost like he knew that’s when the pain was usually at it’s highest of the day. 

 

She rubbed her eye, finding Rio swaying her hips by the kitchen sink. Any other time, Agatha would adore and smile wide at the sight. But when she read the microwave clock to see the fucking time was before six am? 

 

(Five thirty seven, to be exact) 

 

Agatha scoffed. “What the hell?” 

 

Rio jumped, looked over her shoulder with a smile.

 

“Good morning, mi amor!” She beamed. “Coffee is almost ready! Making us some muffins and-”

 

“It’s. Saturday. Rio.” Agatha dramatically stated each word. 


The older woman nodded. “Yes, it is!”

 

“So why the hell are you in the kitchen, high off drugs like you’re in some fucking Disney movie at this god foresaken hour?” 

 

Rio laughed, shaking her head as she gestured outside. 

 

“I have a lot of work ahead of me. Remember? You got me all my supplies”

Rio chuckled, shaking her head. “It’s okay, mi amor. Go back to bed. I’ll be outside working”

When she was more alert, she’d watch Rio in her element. Sip coffee, read a book, enjoy being in the sun as her girlfriend- 

 

No. We aren’t that…not yet. 

 

Rio worked in the garden. For now though, she’d blissfully drift back to sleep to the sound of her lover’s whistling turning into humming, then faint singing. 

 

Agatha smiled to herself. She’s happy.

Music played off her speaker as she hummed along. Sweet Thang, Shuggie Otis. 

 

Calderu coded. 

 

Of course, Rio would pick up music from Lilia. As Agatha grew to learn more about Rio, she saw why the two were good working together and why they got along. Rio had an old soul, she was wise just as Lilia as well.

“Won’t you get bored?”

Has a Saturday ever looked this good?

“Rio” She said.

 

“Yeah?” Rio asked.

 

“Shut up and get back to work” 

 

The older woman paused, but went from nervous to shy. She smiled, nodded as she ran back to where she was working. Agatha focused on her book, Rio played the song over from the beginning as she got her gloves on.

And just like when Rio stretched in front of her…this was worse. Maybe even more than watching her work out. Especially when she had stopped reading, tuned into the grunts between her soft singing. 

 

How her lips would sometimes pull back between her teeth, tongue in cheek. The way her hips would thrust forward and back as she tried to rip the weed from its spot and-

 

“So! You have two gardens?!” 

 

Shit. 

 

Agatha's voice cracked through the question. Her words were frantic, desperate to ignore how hot Rio was making her. Not even the sun could do what she was doing. 

 

Why did I think watching her was a good fucking idea?

Thank fuck. 

 

“Yes- Well..technically three” 

 

Agatha snorted. “Makes sense why you buy the supply list in bulk” 

 

Rio shyly smiled, going back to what she was doing. More than likely assuming the conversation was over. That’s all Agatha cared to learn. 


But then? 

 

“So, how do your three gardens work? What can I expect to see grow?” Agatha asked, turning to rest on her side. Elbow propped up, hand supporting her head. “And do you take requests?”

 

Whoa. 

 

Not just one, nor two, but three questions about her gardens? She was lucky if any ex decided to say hi while she worked, let alone cared to learn about them. 

 

“You really want to know?” Rio asked.

 

“I wanna’ know it all, toots” Agatha winked.

 

Rio visibly looked shocked before nodding, lighting up with every word she said. 

 

“So the front yard, here” She stood, gesturing to it. “These are all my flowers, shrubs, and I’m hoping one day to have an apple tree over there” She pointed. “Make the house look pretty, really”

 

She then gestured to the fence. The exact spot Agatha had crawled and injured herself over. 

 

“Then in the backyard- That’s mainly where I grow my experimental plants. I don’t bring any flowers out here until they grow perfectly and I have the method down. Then my third on the other side of the backyard is where I grow my fruits and vegetables” 

 

Agatha hummed. “So you’ll be my chef from scratch?”

 

“Without a doubt, princess,” Rio winked. 

 

Without a doubt, flirting had made a comeback since that kiss. What surprised Agatha was how extra Rio became with it. She didn’t flirt in a shy way all the time or let Agatha take the reins. She now had a few flirts of her own, winks, names- Especially the newest addition that had become a regular one..

 

Princess.

 

And Agatha really fucking liked it. 

 

She jokingly said it when she brought Agatha her coffee and breakfast. The younger woman had asked for another napkin and when she said thank you? That’s when it happened. 

 

“Anything else, princess?” 

 

Rio must’ve (Without a doubt) seen the way Agatha choked on her eggs. How her skin flushed a deep red. The way she wasn’t able to make eye contact without shivering, burning for a good ten or fifteen minutes. 

 

After that, the name stuck. Rio either used it a couple times a day or saved it when she was bored and wanted to watch Agatha lose her mind a bit.

 

Agatha nodded, clearing her throat to collect herself. 

 

“And what about requests?”

 

Rio was grabbing the rake for the other mess of dead leaves when she turned, head tilted to the side. 

 

“What do you mean?” She asked. 

 

“Like, say I had a flower or food in mind. Would you do it?”

 

Rio leaned, holding the handle of the rake close to her. “Are you serious?”

 

Agatha snorted. “How many more times are you going to ask me that?” 

 

Rio shook her head. If she only knew. 

 

“I’m..sorry- Alright?” Rio chuckled. “This is new. No one cares about this shit. It’s always been me”

 

“Well, I do. So..” Agatha pointed with a tiny smirk. “Get used to it. And also? I've always wanted a pretty garden”

 

Rio snickered. “So you’re saying you’ll be living here one day and bossing me around my garden?”

 

“I’m not technically living here already?” She asked. 

 

“Sprained ankle stay, actually” Rio shrugged.

 

Agatha laughed. It wasn’t just a chuckle, snicker, one of those little snort sounds she made. It was a full on head thrown back type of laugh. One that made Rio’s stomach flutter, her heart soar through the dead garden begging to be brought to life. 

 

Ironic. Rio had spent years bringing life to gardens, plants, every little piece of nature. Yet, no one brought her to life. She lived life for Wanda, Nicky, and most importantly her job. However, everything was still dull. 

 

Then Agatha barged in. From making her life hell to bringing out a new found sense of living in her? 

 

Is this why people love…love? 

 

“Oh, admit it. You’ll still want me when I’m back to jumping and dancing around” Agatha said. 

 

Rio rolled her eyes, pushing the subject back to requests. 

 

“And what would be your request, Agatha?”

 

“Azaleas,” Agatha said. “My favorite flower” 

 

Rio smiled. “Purple, I presume?”

 

“You presume correctly, dear”

 

Rio smiled. She pushed her tongue in her cheek, looking at the garden for where those flowers could go. Her mind instantly thought of the placement. The stone pathway that led from her driveway to the porch. A spot she always wanted to work on, but never got around to it. 

 

“Will those be in the experimental garden first?” Agatha asked. 

 

“No, actually,” Rio said. “I grew them a while ago. Beautiful things” 

 

“They are..” Agatha agreed. “So? Can you?” 

Rio imagined the flowers vividly. How they could create a border on either side of the path. A pretty field of them, leading to her front porch steps. It’d be a piece of Agatha leading her home. 

 

She pulled her lips back, refraining from the lunatic smile she wanted to let go of. 

 

“I can do that” Rio said, looking back to make sure she watched Agatha as she added, “Any more wishes, princess?”

 

And perfect.

 

Her skin under the shade grew redder than the sun could ever burn her. She rushed to grab her book, take her eyes away, clearing her throat dramatically as she shook her head. Rio snickered, not caring if she was heard. The sight was too hysterical, adorable, funny as hell to ignore. 

 

“No- Now, chop chop!” Agatha waved her hand, opening her book. “Get to work!”

 

Rio smirked, nodded, even added a little salute. “Yes ma’am”

Another two weeks. Agatha still was still in pain. 

 

…Or, so Rio thought, anyway. 

 

Rio stumbled down the hallway late one night after falling asleep. She woke up from a bit of commotion, but figured Nicky was just getting water or Agatha had gone to the bathroom. Dressed in a giant shirt down to her knees, rubbing her eye while letting out a yawn-

 

She heard something from the kitchen. 

 

The woman paused, listening closer to the shuffled feet and then noticed the subtle light shadow in the hallway. It was coming from the kitchen, followed by a few beeps signalling the fridge had been open too long. 

 

Rio sighed. Maybe Agatha forgot to close the fridge. That had happened before. Especially when she was tired. The woman was scatter brained enough as it was, tiredness never helped. 

 

She shook her head, muttering under her breath while making her way to the kitchen. Though her annoyance, frustration, tired eyes were swept away by the sight she found. 

 

“Snack time at three am, snack time at three am” 

 

Agatha was holding the fridge open with her hip. Her voice whispered those words in a soft mantra, but added her own singing to it as well. She gave a piece of cheese to Nicky, then herself, then Nicky..and herself. 

 

It wasn’t busting the two for eating late at night, telling Agatha to stop being noisy and go to bed. Rio wasn’t even acknowledging those things. What Rio was focusing on?

 

Agatha’s feet were jumping. She was dancing side to side, having no limping or problem moving on her ankle at all. And instead of being mad how Agatha had milked this, faked the injury for longer than it had been?

 

Rio smirked, arms crossed as she cleared her throat. 


The singing stopped, both turned- Two deers in a pair of headlights. Rio wished in that moment she had her camera. 

 

“So! The ankle is feeling better, I take it?”

 

Agatha stared, forgetting why she was asking until it clicked. Only then did she take a loud gasp, hissed as she tilted away. The fridge door shut behind her, only light in the room from the moon outside. Still bright enough for Rio to watch the dramatic scene before her. 

 

How Agatha dragged her ankle with every step, dropped and slouched in the chair. The cheese was tossed on the table, head tossed back as her eyes squeezed. 

 

“Nope! No, pain. Just…ow”

 

Rio rolled her eyes, unable to keep her smile at bay. “How long have you been better? Also, how long has it been, snack time at three am?” 

 

Agatha looked over, realizing the jig was up. She was busted. Not just her ankle, but her and Nicky’s secret routine. To be fair, the boy played hard. Not like he was going to gain fifty pounds from a little bit of cheese! 

 

That didn’t matter though. Not when Agatha was terrified Rio would want her gone by sunrise. 


Even if they were on the up, only getting better and closer day by day- Agatha didn’t want to leave. Borderline living with Rio had made her the happiest she’d ever been in her whole life! She didn’t want to lose that and had to wait for it to return. 

 

Before Agatha could reply, Rio shook her head with a little smirk. 

 

“Be up for work tomorrow. I’ll drive” 

 

“Wha-”

 

“You’re better. Time for you to be on campus” She said. 

 

Agatha groaned. “No! I’ll go next week”

 

“Ag-”

 

“Listen,” She pointed, sitting up in her chair. “Wanda will be very upset if I miss Thursday lunch tomorrow”

“Don’t lie to me” Rio laughed. 

 

“I’m not! Ask her yourself. She’s bringing subs this time and we even have a movie set up” 

 

Rio huffed. She’d choose her battles with this one. Even though the middle of the night discovery was amusing, she was still too tired to put up with it. 

 

“Fine. Monday morning though, you’re going back” She ordered.

 

“You’ll drive?” Agatha asked. 

 

“Mhm”

 

Agatha lit up, smiling as she asked, “So…I can still be here?” 

 

Who said she could leave?

 

Sure, the original plan was for Agatha’s ankle to heal enough to walk and then the woman would be on her way. That was weeks ago though. Before they spent more time than ever together. All before Rio realized how much she loved going home to Agatha being there, waiting to insult her or pester, annoy in one way or another.

“You’re not leaving” Rio said. 

 

Agatha could die of happiness right then and there.

 

“Guess I can be a patient diagnosed with stockholm syndrome” Agatha mused.

 

Rio snorted. “Oh, totally. You’re very much a victim of a kidnapper in this situation” 

 

“I am” Agatha snickered. “Now, go to bed old woman”

 

Rio was about to ask Agatha to follow. They hadn’t shared a bed since the night in Agatha’s where love confessions turned into days of silence, misunderstanding and poor communication. A reason Rio had been so stand offish. 

 

But now with Agatha staying, how her ankle was better, things were looking up?

 

“Nicky and I were in the middle of a very good movie”

“Limit the cheese, Harkness. We don’t need a fat boy running around” 

 

“So, what are you running around as then?”

“Fuck off, Harkness!” 

 

“Night, Vidal!”

“Want me to bring you something from the restaurant?” 

 

She’d laugh in disbelief. How her best friend and whatever the hell Agatha was now were really hanging out on their own. It made her smile, bite on her bottom lip as her body vibrated with excitement. 

 

Not only was Agatha perfectly melting with her, she was fitting into her life like a puzzle piece. 

 

Nicky adored her. 

Wanda had a new friend to hang out with. 

Natasha seemed to like her as well. 

 

None of her exes ever passed the Natasha test. That was always the hardest. But, Agatha? She passed with flying colors the first time they met. Maybe that should’ve been the sign this was meant to be all along.

And Agatha had no complaints over that. She grew to love working from home. 

 

Rio’s home? Our home? Whatever, she loved being in pajama bottoms and hanging out with Nicky, mid week lunches with Wanda. It was nice. 

 

Alas, her students needed her on campus. Parts of her did miss the classroom, seeing them face to face. She knew Billy was itching to race to her classroom first thing, have lunch with her and help catch her up to speed on all the latest drama (Rio sucked at doing that). It was time to go back. 

 

Especially now with Rio driving and them showing up together. She still wondered how that’d look. What the others would say or do. 

 

Though, Agatha and Rio hadn’t discussed things yet. Would they be out about them? Or just two friends, still enemies, maybe they’d lie how Agatha’s car broke down and Rio was driving her.

Shit.

“Shit”
